本文件按照 GB/T 1.1 一 202 久标准化工作导则第工部分:标准化文件的结构和起草规则的规定起惠。	This document is drafted in accordance with the provisions of GB/T 1.1-202 Standardization Work Guidelines Part I: Structure and Drafting Rules of Standardization Documents.	yes
本文件代替 GB 18030 一 2005 信息技术 ”中文编码字符集与 GB 18030 一 2005 相比,除结构调整和编辑性改动外,主要扩术变化如下:	This document replaces GB 18030-2005 Information technology Chinese coded character set. Compared with GB 18030-2005, except for structural adjustment and editorial changes, the main technical changes are as follows:	yes
增加了本文件适用对象(见第 1 章)，	Adds the applicable object of this document (see Chapter 1),	yes
在双字节编码区更改了 10 个竖排标点和8 个汉字构件所对应的 GB/I 13000 代码位置,并其除了 6 个重复编码的汉字构件和 9 个重复编码的汉字( 见附录 D,2005 年版的附录A)，	In the double-byte coding area, the GB/I 13000 code positions corresponding to 10 vertical punctuation marks and 8 Chinese character components are changed, and 6 repeated coded Chinese character components and 9 repeated coded Chinese characters are removed (see Appendix D, Appendix A of the 2005 edition),	yes
在四字节编码区更改了18 个 GB/T 13000 代码位置(见附录 D,2005 年版的附录D);	18 GB/T 13000 code positions have been changed in the four-byte coding area (see Appendix D, Appendix D of the 2005 edition);	yes
删除了附录 ”追加的汉字及部首/部件 “ 见 2005 年版的附录 〇 ，	Deleted the appendix "Additional Chinese characters and radicals/parts" See appendix D of the 2005 edition,	yes
增加了实现的级别 " (见第9草);	Added implementation level "(see chapter 9);	yes
增加了资料性附录 “通用规范汉字表 ; 议字的代码位置 “ 见附录刁。	Added an informative appendix "Table of General Normative Chinese Characters; Code Positions of Discussed Characters" See Appendix Diao.	yes

GB 18030 一 2022	GB 18030-2022	yes
信息扩术 ”中文编码字符集	Information Expansion Technique "Chinese Coded Character Set	yes
1 本文件规定了信息技术用的中文图形字符及甚二进制编码的十六进制表示 。	1 This document specifies the hexadecimal representation of Chinese graphic characters and even binary codes used in information technology.	yes
本文件适用于中文和其他文字图形字符信息的处理、交换、存储、传给、显现 、输入和输出。	This document applies to the processing, exchange, storage, transmission, display, input and output of Chinese and other graphic character information.	no
本文件适用于为具备中文和其他文字图形字符信息化处理及交换功能的技术类产品,包括但不限于以输入法、光学字符识别 (OCR)、编辑 校对、机融翻诺、语音合成、文字转写、乔能写作等为代表的软件产品 , 以及以计算机、通信终端设备、电子书阅读毅、学习机等为代表的便件产品 。	This document applies to technical products that have the information processing and exchange functions of Chinese and other text and graphic characters, including but not limited to input methods, optical character recognition (OCR), editing and proofreading, machine-integrated translation, speech synthesis, text Transcription, Qiao Neng Writing, etc., as well as convenience products represented by computers, communication terminal equipment, e-book reading devices, learning machines, etc.	no
2 规泄性引用文件	2 Normative references	no
下列文件中的内容通过文中的规范性引用而构成本文件必不可少的条款。	The contents of the following documents constitute the essential provisions of this document through normative references in the text.	no
其中, 注日期的引用文件,仅该日期对应的版本适用于本文件;不注日期的引用文件,其最新厂本(包括所有的修改单)适用于本文件。	Among them, for dated references, only the version corresponding to the date applies to this document; for undated references, the latest version (including all amendments) applies to this document.	no

3 术语和定义	3 Terms and Definitions	no
下列本语和定义适用于本文件 。	The following terms and definitions apply to this document.	no
3.1 字符 character	3.1 Character character	no
供组织、控制或表示数据用的元素集合中的一个元素。	An element in a collection of elements used to organize, control, or represent data.	no
3.2 编码字符 coded character	3.2 Coded character coded character	no
字符 (3.1) 及其编码 示。	Characters (3.1) and their encodings are shown.	no
3.3 用户自定区 private use area	3.3 Private use area	no
使用符合本文件的产品的使用者可以自行规定的区域。	An area that can be specified by the user of a product conforming to this document.	no
3.4 字汇 repertoire	3.4 Repertoire repertoire	no
用编码字符 (3.2) 集表示的一个指定的字符(3.1)集合 。	A specified set of characters (3.1) represented by a coded character (3.2) set.	no

留作未来本文件规定的区 域 。	Area reserved for future provisions of this document.	no
GB 18030 一 2022	GB 18030-2022	no
4 字汇	4 Repertoire	no
4.1 概述	4.1 Overview	no
本文件收录的字符以单字节、双字或四字节编码 。	The characters included in this file are encoded in single-byte, double-word or four-byte.	no
单字节部分收录了 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的 0x00~0x7F 全部 128 个字符 。	The single-byte part contains all 128 characters from 0x00~0x7F of GB/T 11383-1989.	no
4.3 双字节部分	4.3 Double-byte part	no
双字节部分收录了 GB/T 2312 一 1980 中的全部图形字符 GB/T 13000 中的CJK 统一汉字以及部分图形字符。	The double-byte part contains all graphic characters in GB/T 2312-1980, CJK unified Chinese characters and some graphic characters in GB/T 13000.	no
双字节部分的字符按照附录 A 的规定。	The characters in the double-byte part are specified in Appendix A.	no
其中,表意文字描述符的图形、代码位置和功能应符合附录 B 的规定 。	Among them, the graphics, code positions and functions of ideographic descriptors shall comply with the provisions of Appendix B.	no
注: GB/T 13000 对中国、日本、恩国、越南等国家和地区使用的汉字统一编码。	Note: GB/T 13000 is a unified code for Chinese characters used in China, Japan, Korea, Vietnam and other countries and regions.	no
具备独有抽象字形的汉字,赋予单独的代码位置;来源不同而抽象字形相同的汉字, 则赋予共用的代码位置。	Chinese characters with unique abstract glyphs are assigned a separate code position; Chinese characters with different sources but the same abstract glyph are assigned a common code position.	no
经过编码的汉字称为CJK 统一汉字 CCJK Unified Ideographs,其中 CJK 表示中国、日本、韩国。	The encoded Chinese characters are called CJK Unified Ideographs CJK Unified Ideographs, where CJK means China, Japan, and Korea.	no
4.4 四字节部分	4.4 Four-byte part	no
四字节部分收录了上述双字节字符之外的 GB/T 13000 中的 66 个CJK统一汉字(9FA6 一 9FEF，不包括 9FB4~9FBB 的8个字符)、CJK 统一汉字扩充 A、CJK 统一汉字扩充 BCJK 统一汉字扩充 C、 CJK 统一汉字扩充 DCJK 统一汉字扩充下 .CJK 统一汉字扩充 F 和已经 在 GB/ 工 13000 中编码的少数民族文字的字符。	The four-byte part includes 66 CJK Unified Ideographs in GB/T 13000 (9FA6-9FEF, excluding the 8 characters of 9FB4~9FBB), CJK unified Chinese character extension A, CJK unified Chinese character extension BCJK unified Chinese character extension C, CJK unified Chinese character extension DCJK unified Chinese character extension, CJK unified Chinese character extension F and characters of ethnic minorities coded in GB/Work 13000.	no
四字节部分的字符按照附录 C 的规定 。	The characters in the four-byte part are specified in Appendix C.	no
5 总体结构	5 Overall structure	no
正文中凡数字前标有 0x 的表示采用十六进制,未标有 0x 的表示采用十进制。	In the text, the numbers marked with 0x are in hexadecimal notation, and the numbers without 0x are in decimal.	no
附录中凡编码的表示均采用十六进制,其他数字的表示均采用十进制。	All codes in the appendix are expressed in hexadecimal, and other numbers are expressed in decimal.	no
单字节部分采用 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的编码结构,使 用 0x00~0x7F 码位。	The single-byte part adopts the encoding structure of GB/T 11383-1989, using code points 0x00~0x7F.	no
双字贡部分采用两个八位二进制位串表示一个字符,其首字节码位从 0x81 一 0xFE, 尾字节码位分别是 0x40 一 0x7E 和 0x80 一 0xFE。	The double-byte part adopts two eight-bit binary bit strings to represent a character, the code bits of the first byte are from 0x81 to 0xFE, and the code bits of the last byte are 0x40 to 0x7E and 0x80 to 0xFE respectively.	no
四字节部分采用 GB/工 11383 一 1989 未采用的 0x30 一 0x39 作为对双字节编码扩充的后缀,编码范围为 0x81308130 一 0xFE39FE39。	The four-byte part adopts 0x30-0x39 not used in GB/I 11383-1989 as the suffix to expand the double-byte code, and the code range is 0x81308130-0xFE39FE39.	no
四字节字符的第一个字厄编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第二个字记编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39; 第三个字节编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第 四个字市编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39。 即 : 0x81308130 一 0x81308139; 0x81308230 一 0x81308239 0x8130FEFE30 一 0x8130FE39 ; 0x81318130 一 0x81318139 ; Oo2douolag0c “0URo23061393 0xFE39FE30 一 0xFE39FE39 。	The encoding range of the first character of the four-byte character is 0x81-0xFE; the encoding range of the second character is 0x30-0x39; the encoding range of the third byte is 0x81-0xFE; the encoding range of the fourth character is 0x30-0x39. Namely: 0x81308130-0x81308239 0x8130FE30-0x8130FE39; 0x81318130-0x81318139; Oo2douolag0c "0xURo23061393 0x8130FE39FE39.	no
总体结构与码位范围分配见图 1 和表 1。	The overall structure and code point range allocation are shown in Figure 1 and Table 1.	no
6 字符的排列顺序	6 sort order of characters	no
6.1 单字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.1 Arrangement order of single-byte partial characters	no
单字记部分字符按照 GB/I 11383 一 1989 中相应字符的顺序排列 。	Some characters of single-character notes are arranged in the order of corresponding characters in GB/I 11383-1989.	no
6.2 双字市部分字符的排列顺序	6.2 Arrangement order of some characters in double characters	no
双字下部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 A。	The sequence of characters under the double word should be in accordance with Appendix A.	no
6.3 四字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.3 Arrangement order of some characters of four-character brush	no
自 0x81308130 至 0x8439FE39 共 50400 个码位,对应双字节部分未包括的所有 GB/T 13000 基本多文种平面的字符,按照GB/T13000 基本多文种平面相应字符的顺序排列 。	There are a total of 50400 code bits from 0x81308130 to 0x8439FE39, corresponding to all GB/T 13000 Basic Multilingual Plane characters not included in the double-byte part, arranged in the order of the corresponding characters in GB/T 13000 Basic Multilingual Plane.	no
自 0x90308130 至 0xE339FE39 共 1058400 个码位用于对应 GB/T 13000 的16个辅助平面,字符排列顺序完全按照 GB/I 13000 的 16个辅助平面的相应码位顺序依次排列 。	A total of 1,058,400 code bits from 0x90308130 to 0xE339FE39 are used to correspond to the 16 auxiliary planes of GB/T 13000, and the characters are arranged in sequence in accordance with the corresponding code bits of the 16 auxiliary planes of GB/I 13000.	no
四字节部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 C。	The sequence of characters in the four-byte part shall comply with Appendix C.	no

8 部分字符和代码的说明	8 Explanation of some characters and codes	yes
相对于 GB 18030 一 2005 ,部分代码位置上的字形和 /或所对应的 GB/TI 13000 代码位置在本文件中进行了调整 ( 见附录D)。	Compared with GB 18030-2005, the glyphs at some code positions and/or the corresponding GB/TI 13000 code positions have been adjusted in this document (see Appendix D).	yes
9.1 通则	9.1 General	yes
本文件规定三个实现级别。	This document specifies three implementation levels.	yes
符合相应实现级别的系统软件产品,应提供相应实现级别范围内全部字符的输入输出功能。	System software products that meet the corresponding implementation level shall provide input and output functions for all characters within the corresponding implementation level.	yes
9.2 实现级别 1	9.2 Implementation Level 1	yes
实现级别 1 文持本文件的单字节编码部分、双季节编码部分和四字下编玛部分的 CJK 统一汉字 ( 即 0x82358F33 一 0x82359636) 和 CJK 统一汉字扩A( 即 0x8139EE39 一 0x82358738) 。	The level 1 text supports the CJK Unified Ideographs (i.e. 0x82358F33-0x82359636) and CJK Unified Ideographs extension A (i.e. 0x8139EE39-0x82358738) of the single-byte coded part, double-seasonal coded part and four-character subcoded part of this file.	yes
任何本文件适用的产品均应满足实现级别 1 的要求。	Any product to which this document applies shall meet the requirements for Implementation Level 1.	yes
注: 根据软件应用需要 ,实现级别 1 还可选择文持表 3 列出的任何一种或多种非汉字文种。	Note: According to the needs of software applications, implementation level 1 can also choose any one or more non-Chinese characters listed in Table 3.	no
9.3 实现级别 2	9.3 Implementation Level 2	no
实现级别 2 包含实现级别 1。	Implementation level 2 contains implementation level 1.	no
此外 ,实现级别 2 还文持《通用 规范 汉字 表 }中的没有包合在实级别 1 之内的编码汉字。	In addition, the implementation level 2 also supports the coded Chinese characters in the "General Specification Chinese Character Table" that are not included in the actual level 1.	no
《 通用规范汉字表) 所收汉字在本文件中的代码位置和字形, 见附录下。	For the code positions and glyphs of the Chinese characters received in the "General Standard Chinese Character List" in this document, see the appendix.	no
系统软件及支撑软件,应满足实现级别 2 的要求 。	System software and supporting software shall meet the requirements of level 2.	no
注: 系统软件及文撑软件包括但不限于操作系统,数据库管理系统.中间件( 软件产品分类的信息见 GB/ 工 36475)。	Note: System software and supporting software include but not limited to operating system, database management system, and middleware (see GB/Work 36475 for information on software product classification).	no
9.4 实现级别 3	9.4 Implementation Level 3	no
实现级别 3 包含实现级别 2。	Implementation level 3 contains implementation level 2.	no
此外,实现级别 3 还文持本文件规定的全部汉字及表 3 中的康黑部首。	In addition, the implementation level 3 also supports all the Chinese characters specified in this document and the Kanghe radicals in Table 3.	no
用于政务服务和公共服务的产品应满足实现级卉 3 的要求。	Products used for government services and public services should meet the requirements of level 3.	no
注: 政务服务和 共服务行业包括但不限于铁路运输业.道路运输业 \ 水上运输业.航空运输业、多式联运和运输代理业、邮政业、货币金融服、保险业、土地、管理业、卫生、国家机构、社会保障等 (行业分类的信息见 GB/ 工 4754)。	Note: Government services and public service industries include but are not limited to railway transportation, road transportation, water transportation, air transportation, multimodal transportation and transportation agency, postal service, monetary and financial services, insurance, land, management, health, state agencies, social security, etc. (see GB/Work 4754 for industry classification information).	no

描述 (DESCRIPTION) C 和 C++ 编译器是集成的.他们都要用四个步骤中的一个或多个处理输入文件: 预处理(preprocessing), Hii(compilation), (assembly) MERE (linking) .	DESCRIPTION (DESCRIPTION) The C and C++ compilers are integrated. They both process input files in one or more of four steps: preprocessing (preprocessing), Hii (compilation), (assembly) MERE (linking).	yes
源文件后级名标识源文件的语言, 但是对编译器来说, 后绥名控制着缺省设定:	The source file suffix identifies the language of the source file, but as far as the compiler is concerned, the suffix controls the default setting:	yes
gcc 认为预处理后的文件(.i) 是 c 文件, 并且设定 c 形式的连接，	gcc considers the preprocessed file (.i) to be a c file, and sets the link in c form,	yes

在连接阶段中,所有对应于源程序的.e 文件，-1 库文件, 无法识别的文件名(包括指定的.o H 标文件和 .a 库文件)按命令行中的顺序传递给连接器选项 (OPTIONS)	In the connection phase, all .e files corresponding to source programs, -1 library files, and unrecognized file names (including specified .o H standard files and .a library files) are passed to the linker in the order in the command line OPTIONS	no
选项必须分立给出 : de ' 完全不同于 `-d -r '.	Options must be given separately: de 'is completely different from '-d -r '.	no
大多数 ` -=E :和 `-W' 选项有两个相反的格式 : -fname 和 -fno-name (或 -Wname 和 -Wno- name).	Most '-=E: and '-W' options have two opposite forms: -fname and -fno-name (or -Wname and -Wno-name).	no
这里只列举不是默认选项的格式.	Only formats that are not the default options are listed here.	no

明确指出后面输入文件的语言为 language (而不是从文件名后绥得到的默认选择).	Explicitly indicate that the language of subsequent input files is language (instead of the default selection from the filename suffix).	yes
这个选项应用于后面所有的输入文件, 直到遇着下一个 `-x' 选项 .language 的可选	This option applies to all subsequent input files until the next '-x' option .language optional	yes
关闭任何对语种的明确说明, 因此依据文件名后级处理后面的文件 RE AS E ` -x' 选项).	Turn off any explicit specification of the language, so subsequent files are processed according to the file name RE AS E '-x' option).	yes
如果只操作四个阶段( 预处理, 编译, 汇编, 连接)中的一部分, 可以使用 ` -x' 选项 (或文件名后 Ah) 告诉 geo 从哪里开始,用 `~-c' ，`-s' ,或 `-E' 选项告诉 geo 到哪里结束.注意,某些选项组合 (例如 ，`-x cpp-output -E') {i gee MEF =c 编译或汇编源文件, ETER. ERA ATI 缺省情况下， GCC 通过用 ` .o' 蔡换源文件名后级 ` .ec 标文件名. 可以使用-o 选项选择其他名字.GCC忽略 -ec 选项后面任何无法识别的输入文伯 -S F 何事情.	If you only operate part of the four stages (preprocessing, compiling, assembling, linking), you can use the '-x' option (or Ah after the file name) to tell geo where to start, use '~-c', '-s', or the '-E' option tells geo where to end. Note that some combinations of options (for example, '-x cpp-output -E') {i gee MEF =c compile or assemble source files, ETER. ERA ATI By default, GCC replaces source file names with '.o' followed by '.ec'. Other names can be selected using the -o option.	yes
了的目标文件.	the target file.	yes
编译后即停止, 不进行汇编件.	Stops after compiling, no assembly is performed.	yes
在编译过程的不同阶段间使用管道而非临时文件进行工作, 因为那些系统的汇编器不能从管道读取数据，GNU 的汇编器没有这个问题，汇编器能够接受的 C "方言 ": 支持符合 ANSI 标准的 C 程序.	Use pipes instead of temporary files to work between different stages of the compilation process, because the assemblers on those systems cannot read from pipes. The GNU assembler does not have this problem. C "dialects" accepted by assemblers: Support ANSI compliant C programs.	yes
这样就会关闭 GNU Cc 中某些不兼容 ANSI Cc 的特性关键字, 以及诸如 unix 和 vax 这些表明当迎和极少使用的 ANSI trigraph 特性,以及禁上尽管使 用了(译注 :宿主环境 (hosted environment) 下所有的标准库可用，main 函数返回 一个 int 值, 典型例子是除了内核以外几乎所有的程序.对应的独立环境 (f£reestanding environment) 不存在标准库, 程序入口也不一定是 main, 最明显的例子就是操作系统内核.详情参考 gcc 网站最近的资料)	This will turn off some of the feature keywords in GNU Cc that are not compatible with ANSI Cc, as well as the ANSI trigraph features such as unix and vax that are denoted as welcome and rarely used, and even if used (Note: Hosted environment (hosted environment) is available in all standard libraries, the main function returns an int value, a typical example is almost all programs except the kernel. The corresponding independent environment (f£reestanding environment) does not exist in the standard library, and the program entry is not necessarily main, the most obvious example is the operating system kernel. For details, refer to the latest information on the gcc website)	yes
对于没有参数的函数声明, 例如 `int foo ();', 按 C 风格处理 --- 即不说明参数个数或类型. (仅针对 C++) .	For function declarations without parameters, such as'int foo ();', treat them C-style --- that is, do not specify the number or types of parameters. (C++ only).	no
正常情况下, 这样的函数 foo 在 C++ 中意味着参数为空.	Normally, such a function foo means in C++ that the argument is empty.	no
节清单从这里删到试图支持传统 C 编译器的某些方面.	Section listings are cut here to try to support some aspects of traditional C compilers.	no
详见NU c 手册,我们已经把细节删除, 这样当内容过时后, 人们也不会 HERI.	See the NU c manual for details, we've removed the details so that people don't HERI when the content becomes obsolete.	no
除了一件事: 对于 c++ 程序 (不是C)，` -traditional' 选项带来一个附加效应,允许对 this 赋值.	Except for one thing: for c++ programs (not C), the '-traditional' option has the added effect of allowing assignment to this.	no
他和`-Ethis-is-variable' 选项的果一样.	It has the same effect as the '-Ethis-is-variable' option.	no
-traditional-cpp 试图支持传统 Cc 预处理器的某些方面.	-traditional-cpp Attempts to support some aspects of the traditional Cc preprocessor.	no
特别是上面提到有关预处理器的内容, 但是不包括 `-traditional' 选项的其他效应.	Specifically what is mentioned above about the preprocessor, but not other effects of the '-traditional' option.	no
-fdollars-in-identifiers 允许在标识符 (identifier) 中使用 `$' 字符 (仅针对 C++) .	-fdollars-in-identifiers Allow '$' characters in identifiers (C++ only).	no
你可以指定 `“-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' 选项显明禁止使用 `$' 符.	You can specify the '"-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' option to explicitly disable the '$' character.	no
(GNU C++ 在某些目标系统缺省允许 `$' 符, 但不是所有系统.)	(GNU C++ allows the '$' character by default on some target systems, but not all.)	no
-fenum-int-equiv 允许 ant 类型到枚举类型 (enumeration) 的隐式转换 (MEF c++) .	-fenum-int-equiv Allow implicit conversion of ant types to enumeration types (MEF c++).	no
正常情况下 GNU C++ 允许从 enum 到 int 的转换,反之则不行.	Normally GNU C++ allows conversion from enum to int, but not vice versa.	no
-fexternal-—templates 为模板声明 (template declaration) 产生较小的代码 (仅限于 c++)，方法是对于每个模板函数 (template function),只在 定义他们的地方生成一个副本.	-fexternal--templates Generate smaller code (c++ only) for template declarations by, for each template function, making a copy only where they are defined.	no
想要成功使用这个选项, 你必须在所有使用模板的文件中,标记`#pragma implementatio'(定义)或 `#Pragma interface'(声明).	To successfully use this option, you must mark '#pragma implementatio' (definition) or '#Pragma interface' (declaration) in all files using templates.	no
程序用 `-fexternal-templates ' 编译时, 模板实例 (template instantiation) 全部是外部类型.你必须让需要的实例在实现文件中出现.	When a program is compiled with '-fexternal-templates ', template instantiations are all external types. You must make the required instances appear in the implementation file.	no
可以通过 typedef 实现这一点, 他引用所需的每个实例.	This can be achieved with typedefs, which refer to each instance needed.	no
相对应的, 如果编译时使用缺省选项 ` -fno-exteznal-templates', 所有模板实例明确的设为内置.	Correspondingly, when compiling with the default '-fno-exteznal-templates' option, all template instances are explicitly set as built-ins.	no
所有的成员函数(除了构造子函数和 mnew 或 delete 成员操作符) 视为所在类的虚函数.	All member functions (except constructor functions and the mnew or delete member operators) are treated as virtual functions of the enclosing class.	no
这不表明每次调用成员函数都将通过内部虚函数表.	This does not mean that every call to a member function will go through the internal virtual function table.	no
有些情况下, 编译器能够判断出可以直接调用某个虚函数; 这时就直接调用.	In some cases, the compiler can determine that a virtual function can be called directly; in this case, it will be called directly.	no
-fcond-mismatch 允许条件表达式的第二和第三个参数的类型不匹配.	-fcond-mismatch Allow type mismatch between the second and third arguments of the condition expression.	no
这种表达式的值是 Void.-fthis-—is-variable 允许对 this 赋值 (仅对 c++).	The value of such an expression is Void. -fthis--is-variable allows assignment to this (c++ only).	no
合并用户自定义的自由存储管理机制到 c++ 后,使可赋值的`this' 显得不合时宜.	Incorporating user-defined free storage management into C++ made assignable'this' anachronistic.	no
因此, 默认情况下, 类成员函数内部对 this 赋值是无效操作.	Therefore, by default, assignment to this inside a class member function is an invalid operation.	no
然而为了向后兼容, 你可以通过 `-fthis-is-variable' 选项使这种操作有效.	However, for backwards compatibility, you can enable this with the '-fthis-is-variable' option.	no
-funsigned-char 把 char 定义为无符号类型,如同 unsigned char.	-funsigned-char Define char as an unsigned type, like unsigned char.	no
各种机器都有自己缺省的 char 类型. 既可能是 unsigned char 也可能是 signed char.	Various machines have their own default char type. It may be unsigned char or signed char.	no
理想情况下, 当依赖于数据的符号性时, 一个可移植程序总是应该使用 signed char 或 unsigned chaz.	Ideally, a portable program should always use signed char or unsigned chaz when relying on the signedness of the data.	no
但是许多程序已经写成只用简单的 char, 并且期街这是有符号数(或者无符号数, 具体情况取决于编写程序的目标机器).	But many programs have been written to use only plain char, and expect this to be signed (or unsigned, depending on the machine the program is written for).	no
这个选项, 和它的反义选项, 使那样的程序工作在对应的默认值上.	This option, and its inverse, make that program work on the corresponding default.	no
char 的类型始终应该明确定义为 signed char 或 unsigned char, 即使它表现的和其中之一完全一样.	The type of char should always be explicitly defined as either signed char or unsigned char, even if it behaves exactly like one of them.	no
如果没有明确声明 ` signed' 或 "unsigned'修饰符, 这些选项用来定义有符号位域 (bitfield) 或无符号位域.	If no'signed' or "unsigned' modifiers are explicitly specified, these options are used to define signed or unsigned bitfields.	no
缺省情况下,位域是有符号的, 因为他们继承的基本整数类型,如 int,是有符号数，然而, 如果指定了 `-traditional' 选项,位域永远是无符号数.	By default, bitfields are signed, because the underlying integer types they inherit from, such as int, are signed, however, if the '-traditional' option is specified, bitfields are always unsigned.	no
-fwritable-strings把字符串常量存储到可写数据段, 而且不做特别对待.	-fwritable-strings Store string constants in the writable data segment, and do not treat them specially.	no
这是为了兼容一些老程序,他们算改字符串常量是一个非常糟糕的想法、`-traditional' 选项也有相同效果.	This is for compatibility with older programs, who consider changing string constants to be a very bad idea. The '-traditional' option has the same effect.	no
执行摘要	executive summary	yes
新冠肺炎对毒品市场的影响	Impact of COVID-19 on drug markets	yes
其影响可能类似于2008年的经济危机	The impact could be similar to the 2008 economic crisis	yes
全球性的新冠肺炎疫情已使全世界陷入前所未有的危机。	The global COVID-19 pandemic has plunged the world into an unprecedented crisis.	yes
在许多国家，这一疾病己使医疗服务机构穷于应付，几近崩溃，各国政府实施的限制措施已在全球经济中造成了严重紊乱。	In many countries, the disease has overwhelmed health services to the point of collapse, and restrictions imposed by governments have caused severe disruption in the global economy.	yes
对于毒品市场，这场疫情的影响尚不清楚，也很难预测，但有可能影响深远。	For the drug market, the impact of the outbreak is unclear and difficult to predict, but could be far-reaching.	yes
一些生产者可能会被迫寻找新的方法来制造毒品，因为限制流动的同时也限制了前体和基本化学品的获取。	Some producers may be forced to find new ways to manufacture drugs, as restrictions on movement also limit access to precursors and essential chemicals.	yes
贩运者由于旅行限制而无法越境，可能不得不寻找新的路线和方法。	Traffickers, unable to cross borders due to travel restrictions, may have to find new routes and methods.	yes
毒品使用和提供的模式可能会改变，政府的应对能力也可能会受到阻碍。	Patterns of drug use and availability may change, and governments' ability to respond may be hampered.	yes
新冠肺炎带来的转变是前所未有的，但还是可以从以往的危机中吸取一些经验教训。	The shift brought about by COVID-19 is unprecedented, but there are some lessons that can be learned from previous crises.	yes
2008年经济危机后，一些吸毒者开始寻找更便宜的合成物质，使用模式转向注射毒品。	After the 2008 economic crisis, some drug users began to seek out cheaper synthetic substances, and usage patterns shifted to injecting drugs.	no
与此同时，各国政府削减了与毒品相关的预算。	At the same time, governments have cut drug-related budgets.	no
如果各国政府以同样的方式应对当前的经济衰退，预防吸毒和相关风险行为等干预措施和戒毒治疗服务可能会受到沉重打击。	If governments responded to the current recession in the same way, interventions such as prevention of drug use and related risk behaviors and drug treatment services could be hit hard.	no
此外，拦截行动和国际合作的优先性可能会降低，使贩运者更容易行动。	In addition, interdiction operations and international cooperation may be lowered in priority, making it easier for traffickers to operate.	no
一些国家有大量毒品通过商业航班走私，预计这些国家的贩毒活动受到的直接影响最大。	Drug trafficking is expected to be most directly affected in countries where large quantities of drugs are smuggled via commercial flights.	no
有信使将甲基苯丙胺等合成毒品放在随身背包或藏在私人行李中携带，有时数量很大。由于几乎各地都对航空客运实施了限制，利用商业航空旅行供应毒品的活动可能会完全中断。	Couriers carry synthetic drugs such as methamphetamine in carry-on backpacks or concealed in personal luggage, sometimes in large quantities. The use of commercial air travel to supply drugs could be completely disrupted as restrictions on air passenger traffic are imposed almost everywhere.	no
尽管国际邮政供应链也受到了干扰，但利用暗网和货物邮寄进行贩运的活动可能会增加。	While international postal supply chains have also been disrupted, there is likely to be an increase in trafficking using the darknet and postal delivery of goods.	no
从长远来看，经济衰退和相关的封闭措施可能会打乱毒品市场。	In the long run, the recession and associated lockdowns could disrupt the drug market.	no
由于不断上升的失业率和缺乏机会，贫困和弱势人群将更有可能以有害的方式吸毒，患上吸毒病症，并转向与毒品有关的非法活动一无论是生产还是运输。	As a result of rising unemployment and lack of opportunity, the poor and vulnerable will be more likely to use drugs in harmful ways, develop drug use disorders, and turn to illicit drug-related activities - whether producing or transporting them.	no
贩毒组织可能会利用这种情况，向脆弱人群提供服务，并招募新成员来壮大队伍。	Drug trafficking organizations may take advantage of this situation by providing services to vulnerable populations and recruiting new members to bolster their ranks.	no
随着政府应对能力的降低，这些转变可能会快速扎根，成为许多社区的新现实。	With reduced government capacity to respond, these shifts could quickly take hold as the new reality for many communities.	no
扩张与复杂性	Expansion and Complexity	no
市场增长	market growth	no
人口增长模式部分解释了市场扩张的原因	Population Growth Patterns partly Explain Market Expansion	no
世界各地的吸毒现象一直在增多，无论是从总体数字还是从吸毒者在世界人口中所占比例来看都是如此。	Drug use has been increasing around the world, both in overall figures and as a percentage of the world's population who use drugs.	no
2009年估计吸毒者有2.1亿人，占全球15-64岁人口的4.8%,而2018年估计吸毒者有2.69亿人，占这类人口的5.3%。	In 2009 there were an estimated 210 million drug users, or 4.8% of the global population aged 15-64, while in 2018 there were an estimated 269 million drug users, or 5.3% of this population.	no
在过去二十年期间，发展中国家吸毒情况的增长速度远远快于发达国家。	During the past two decades, drug use has grown much faster in developing countries than in developed countries.	no
这在一定程度上反映了这一期间总体人口增长的差异、发达国家为7%,发展中国家为28%但也反映了发展中国家年 轻人口增长较快。	This partly reflects differences in overall population growth over the period, 7 per cent in developed countries and 28 per cent in developing countries, but also reflects faster growth in younger populations in developing countries.	no
青少年和年轻成年人在吸毒者中所占比例最大。	Adolescents and young adults make up the largest proportion of drug users.	no
在2000-2018年期间，发展中国家这一年龄段的人口增长了16%,而发达国家这一年龄段的人口减少了10%。	During the period 2000-2018, the population of this age group in developing countries grew by 16%, while in developed countries it decreased by 10%.	no
1城市化是当前和未来毒品市场的一个驱动因素	1 Urbanization is a driver of current and future drug markets	no
无论是发达国家还是发展中国家，城市地区的吸毒情况都多于农村地区。	Drug use is more common in urban areas than in rural areas, both in developed and developing countries.	no
吸毒情况总体增多的部分原因是人口从农村向城镇的大规模流动一目前全世界人口有一半以上生活在城市地区，而1960年这一比例为34%。	The overall increase in drug use is partly due to the massive movement of people from rural to urban areas - more than half of the world's population now lives in urban areas, compared with 34 per cent in 1960.	no
城市化可能是毒品市场未来动态的一个关键因素，特别是在城市化趋势更为突出的发展中国家。	Urbanization may be a key factor in the future dynamics of drug markets, especially in developing countries where urbanization tends to be more pronounced.	no
财富的增加与吸毒情况增多相联，但承受疾病负担最大的是最贫穷的人在世界范围内，发达国家的吸毒情况比发展中国家更为普遍。	Increased wealth is associated with increased drug use, but the burden of disease is greatest among the poorest Worldwide, drug use is more prevalent in developed countries than in developing countries.	no
可卡因之类的毒品更是与世界上较富裕的地区联系较为牢固。	Drugs such as cocaine are more strongly associated with wealthier parts of the world.	no
同样，在各国内部，社会富裕阶层的吸毒流行率较高。	Likewise, within countries, the prevalence of drug use is higher among wealthier segments of society.	no
但转为吸毒病症的比率较高的却是社会经济地位较低的人。	However, the higher rates of transition to substance use disorders are among those of lower socioeconomic status.	no
来自少数几个国家的数据表明，有害的吸毒模式与病症同低收入之间存在联系。	Data from a handful of countries show a link between harmful drug use patterns and conditions and low income.	no
这些模式在较富裕的社会阶层似乎不太常见。	These patterns appear to be less common in wealthier social classes.	no
全球新冠肺炎危机造成的经济制约很可能会加剧包括吸毒者在内的最弱势群体的风险。	The economic constraints imposed by the global COVID-19 crisis are likely to exacerbate the risks for the most vulnerable groups, including drug users.	no
例如，劳动力市场的变化，如失业率上升，过去一直与吸毒情况的增加有关，而这场疫情己经迫使全球数千万人失业。	For example, changes in the labor market, such as rising unemployment, have been linked in the past to increased drug use, and the pandemic has forced tens of millions of people out of work around the world.	no
新冠肺炎或将导致毒品市场进一步扩张新冠肺炎的大流行可能会导致更多农民增加或从事非法作物种植，或是因为国家主管机关的控制能力降低，或是因为在经济危机之下可能有更多人不得不铤而走险，从事非法活动。	COVID-19 may lead to further expansion of drug market The COVID-19 pandemic may lead to more farmers to increase or engage in illicit crops, either because the control capacity of national authorities is reduced, or because in the economic crisis more people may have to take risks and engage in illegal activities.	no
新冠肺炎的相关限制措施导致空中和陆路交通减少，海上贩运可能已经因此而增加，海上的拦截风险低，而且比空中或陆路走私的数量更多。	Trafficking by sea may have increased as a result of reduced air and land traffic due to COVID-19-related restrictions, where the risk of interception is low and higher volumes are smuggled than by air or land.	no
最近已有报告称可卡因货物直接从南美经由海路运往欧洲。	Recently there have been reports of shipments of cocaine directly from South America to Europe by sea.	no
复杂性增强	Increased complexity	yes
非国际管制物质的出现情况稳定，但有潜在危害的新型类阿片正在增多毒品市场正日趋复杂。	The presence of substances not under international control is stable, but new and potentially harmful opioids are on the rise The drug market is becoming more complex.	yes
除大麻、可卡因和海洛因等植物类物质之外，已经增添了数百种合成毒品，其中许多并不在国际管制之下。药品的非医疗使用也快速增多。	To the plant-based substances such as marijuana, cocaine and heroin, hundreds of synthetic drugs have been added, many of which are not under international control. The non-medical use of medicines is also rapidly increasing.	yes
会员国的国内市场每年约有500种新型活性物质。	There are about 500 new active substances per year on the domestic market of Member States.	yes
目前其中大多是兴奋剂，其次是合成的大麻素受体激动剂和少量的类阿片。	Most of these are currently stimulants, followed by synthetic cannabinoid receptor agonists and a small amount of opioids.	yes
虽然新型精神活性物质的总体数量已经稳定下来，但比例发生了变化。	While the overall number of NPS has stabilized, the proportions have changed.	yes
在2014年确定的新型精神活性物质种类总数中，类阿片新型精神活性物质仅占2%,但到2018年，这一数字己上升至9%。	Opioid NPS accounted for only 2% of the total number of NPS identified in 2014, but by 2018 this figure had risen to 9%.	yes
类阿片新型精神活性物质中有许多是芬太尼的类似物，其药效和危害已得到证明，在北美导致了过量死亡事件，其他区域也有，但程度较轻。	The NPS opioids, many of which are analogues of fentanyl, have proven efficacy and harm, leading to overdose deaths in North America and, to a lesser extent, elsewhere.	yes
在北美，芬太尼有的用作海洛因和其他毒品（包括可卡因和甲基苯丙胺）的掺杂剂，有的用来制造假冒的药用类阿片。	In North America, fentanyl is used either as a doping agent for heroin and other drugs, including cocaine and methamphetamine, or to manufacture counterfeit pharmaceutical opioids.	yes
一些证据表明，欧洲也有注射新型精神活性物质兴奋剂的现象：一项对欧洲六个城市废弃注射器残留物的研宄发现，许多注射器都沾有产生兴奋作用的新型精神活性物质》	There is some evidence that injecting NPS stimulants also occurs in Europe: A study of the residues of discarded syringes in six European cities finds that many are stained with NPS that produce stimulants"	yes
2新型精神活性物质的使用可能会逐渐牢固存在于弱势群体中	2 The use of new psychoactive substances may become firmly established in vulnerable groups	no
单一种类的新型精神活性物质几乎从未形成大的市场。	A single class of NPS almost never forms a large market.	no
但来自欧洲的证据表明，合成大麻素在无家可归者和监狱囚犯等社会边缘群体中是一个严重的问题。	But evidence from Europe suggests that synthetic cannabinoids are a serious problem among socially marginalized groups such as the homeless and prison inmates.	no
有22个国家报告了监狱中使用新型精神活性物质的情况，其中大多数国家将合成大麻素确定为主要挑战。	Twenty-two countries reported on the use of NPS in prisons, most of which identified synthetic cannabinoids as a major challenge.	no
对前体化学品的管制迫使制毒者进行创新最常作为前体用来合成苯丙胺、甲基苯丙胺和“摇头丸”等毒品的许多化学品已被置于国际管制之下。	Control of precursor chemicals forces drugmakers to innovate Many of the chemicals most commonly used as precursors in the synthesis of drugs such as amphetamine, methamphetamine and "ecstasy" have been placed under international control.	no
贩毒者和制毒者一直在寻找替代品一不仅有管制较松的物质，还有专门为规避管制而设计的化学品，即所谓的“特制前体”。	Drug traffickers and producers are always looking for alternatives - not just less regulated substances, but also chemicals specifically designed to circumvent them, so-called "designer precursors."	no
旨在阻止新冠肺炎传播的限制性措施很可能使依赖前体化学品的制毒者受到进一步挤压。	Restrictive measures aimed at halting the spread of COVID-19 are likely to further squeeze drug makers who rely on precursor chemicals.	no
来自墨西哥的证据表明，这已经成为 现实：据报告，2020年3月，从东亚进口的甲基苯丙胺前体短缺促使墨西哥和美国的甲基苯丙胺价格上涨。	Evidence from Mexico suggests that this is already a reality: in March 2020, shortages of methamphetamine precursors imported from East Asia were reported to have contributed to increases in methamphetamine prices in Mexico and the United States.	no
市场瞬息万变	The market is changing rapidly	no
合成药物在中亚和俄罗斯联邦取代阿片剂	Synthetic drugs replacing opiates in Central Asia and the Russian Federation	no
中亚和俄罗斯联邦的阿片剂市场在2008年至2018年期间似乎发生了变化。	The opiate market in Central Asia and the Russian Federation appears to have changed between 2008 and 2018.	no
俄罗斯联邦当局截获的阿片剂数量下降了约80%，同时因使用类阿片而接受治疗的人数大幅减少。	The number of opiates intercepted by Russian Federation authorities has fallen by about 80%, while the number of people receiving treatment for opioid use has dropped significantly.	no
但兴奋剂市场却似乎日渐兴旺。	But the doping market seems to be thriving.	no
有证据表明，甲基苯丙胺和各种卡西酮，包括甲氧麻黄酮和 a - 吡咯烷基苯戊酮，现在俄罗斯毒品市场上随处可见。	There is evidence that methamphetamine and various cathinones, including mephedrone and a-pyrrolidinylvalerone, are now ubiquitous on the Russian drug market.	no
俄罗斯当局报告称，最近查获的制造各种非法药物的秘密加工点数量急剧上升，在两年内翻了一番多，2018年增至152个加工点。	Russian authorities reported a sharp rise in recent seizures of clandestine laboratories manufacturing a variety of illicit drugs, more than doubling in two years to 152 laboratories in 2018.	no
阿富汗和伊拉克甲基苯丙胺市场增长	Methamphetamine market growth in Afghanistan and Iraq	no
早在2012年，对医院、监狱和其他机构人员的调查就已经揭示了甲基苯丙胺在伊拉克的重要性。	As early as 2012, investigations of personnel in hospitals, prisons and other institutions had revealed the importance of methamphetamine in Iraq.	no
结晶甲基苯丙胺已经成为“芬乃他林”和曲马多之外又一种令人担忧的主要药物。	Crystalline methamphetamine has become a major drug of concern alongside "captagon" and tramadol.	no
2015年的一项研宄进一步证实了这些发现，吸毒者表示大麻比“芬乃他林”或甲基苯丙胺更难获得。	A 2015 study reinforced these findings, with drug users saying marijuana was more difficult to obtain than "captagon" or methamphetamine.	no
最近，伊拉克当局发现了多个甲基苯丙胺加工点，麻管局已对伪麻黄碱制剂的大批进口表示关切一甲基苯丙胺加工点将这些制剂用作前体。	More recently, the Iraqi authorities have discovered methamphetamine laboratories, and the Board has expressed concern about the importation of large quantities of pseudoephedrine preparations, which are used as precursors by methamphetamine laboratories.	no
在阿富汗，甲基苯丙胺制造似乎始于2014年。	In Afghanistan, methamphetamine manufacture appears to have begun in 2014.	no
自那时起，甲基苯丙胺的缉获量一直在稳步上升。	Seizures of methamphetamine have been steadily rising since then.	no
但2019年上半年的缉获量一^657公斤——与上一年相比大幅骤增。	But seizures in the first half of 2019 totaled 657kg - a sharp jump from the previous year.	no
在其他国家大量缉获了据认为源自阿富汗的甲基苯丙胺，这也表明该国的产量正在迅速上升。	Large seizures in other countries of methamphetamine thought to have originated in Afghanistan also suggest that production in that country is rapidly rising.	no
政策变化和变化趋势	Policy Changes and Trends	yes
非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域大多有大麻使用增多的趋势	Jurisdictions that have legalized non-medical use of cannabis show a trend towards increased cannabis use	yes
加拿大、乌拉圭和美国的11个法域允许制造大麻产品供非医疗使用。	Eleven jurisdictions in Canada, Uruguay and the United States allow the manufacture of cannabis products for non-medical use.	yes
在其中多数法域，大麻使用自合法化以来有所增多，尽管在其他未将非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域也观察到了同样的趋势。	In most of these jurisdictions, cannabis use has increased since legalization, although the same trend has been observed in other jurisdictions that have not legalized the non-medical use of cannabis.	yes
在美国最早通过立法的两个州科罗拉多州和华盛顿州，成年人非医疗使用大麻的情况增加，特别是过去一个月以及每天或几乎每天使用的情况增多，自2012年起便已超过了全国平均水平。	In Colorado and Washington, two of the first U.S. states to pass legislation, non-medical use of marijuana among adults has increased, particularly in the past month and daily or near-daily use, exceeding the national average since 2012 level.	yes
所有指标都显示，自2011年以来，乌拉圭的大麻使用情况有所增加，上月使用情况几乎翻了一番。	All indicators show that cannabis use has increased in Uruguay since 2011, with use almost doubling in the last month.	yes
这表明增加的主要原因是经常和频繁使用大麻。	This suggests that the main reason for the increase is regular and frequent cannabis use.	yes
加拿大的短期数据也表明，2018年至2019年合法市场扩大的同时，使用量也在增加。	Short-term data from Canada also show that the legal market expanded from 2018 to 2019 while usage increased.	yes
然而，2019年仍有40%的大麻使用者靠非法来源获得某些产品。	However, 40% of cannabis users in 2019 still obtained some products from illicit sources.	yes
全球大麻药草缉获量暴跌的背后原因是大麻合法化？	Is marijuana legalization behind plummeting global marijuana herb seizures?	yes
2018年，全球大麻药草缉获量降至20年来的最低水平，这是因为北美的缉获量下降，在过去10年中下降了 84%。	Global seizures of cannabis herb fell to their lowest level in 20 years in 2018, as seizures in North America fell, falling by 84% over the past 10 years.	no
相比之下，同期世界其他地区的缉获量几乎翻了一番。缉获的模式表明，旨在放开大麻市场的政策在下降中发挥了关键作用。	In contrast, seizures in other parts of the world almost doubled during the same period. The pattern of seizures suggests that policies aimed at liberalizing the marijuana market played a key role in the decline.	no
对新型精神活性物质的监管似乎有遏制作用在国内对新型精神活性物质的监管效果仍然很难评估。	Regulation of NPS appears to have a deterrent effect The domestic regulation of NPS remains difficult to assess.	no
一些对新型精神活性物质采用不同监管制度的国家显示出不同的新型精神活性物质使用流行率。	Some countries with different regulatory regimes for NPS show different prevalence of NPS use.	no
在另一些国家，通过国内立法后，新型精神活性物质使用情况有所减少。	In other countries, the use of NPS has decreased following the adoption of domestic legislation.	no
弱势群体面临合法和非法毒品市场的伤害用于疼痛管理和姑息治疗的药用类阿片主要在高收入国家提供止痛药在各区域分布不均。	Vulnerable populations face harm from legal and illicit drug markets Pharmaceutical opioids for pain management and palliative care are mainly available in high-income countries Pain relief is unevenly distributed across regions.	no
2018年，所有可供医疗消费的药用类阿片中，90%以上在高收入国家。	In 2018, more than 90 per cent of all pharmaceutical opioids available for medical consumption were in high-income countries.	no
大约50%在北美，40%在欧洲，还有2%在大洋洲。	About 50% are in North America, 40% in Europe, and 2% in Oceania.	no
这些国家的人口约占全球人口的12%。	These countries account for approximately 12% of the global population.	no
据估计，低收入和中等收入国家的人口占全球人口的88%,但消费的药用类阿片却不到10%。	It is estimated that low- and middle-income countries, home to 88% of the global population, consume less than 10% of pharmaceutical opioids.	no
获取药用类阿片的障碍与许多因素有关，包括立法、文化、卫生系统和处方做法。	Barriers to access to pharmaceutical opioids are related to many factors, including legislation, culture, health systems and prescribing practices.	no
较贫穷的人患吸毒病症的风险更大2018年约有3,560万人患有吸毒病症。	Poorer people are at greater risk of developing a substance use disorder Some 35.6 million people suffered from a substance use disorder in 2018.	no
贫困、有限的教育和社会边缘化可能会增加吸毒病症风险，并加剧其后果。高收入国家的研宄证实了这一点，在这些研究中，个人不利的社会经济轨迹一不仅仅是他们在某一时间点的状况一也与吸毒病症风险有关。	Poverty, limited education and social marginalization may increase the risk of substance use disorders and exacerbate their consequences. This is confirmed by studies in high-income countries where individuals' unfavorable socioeconomic trajectories - not just their status at a certain point in time - are also associated with drug use disorder risk.	no
吸毒病症还会加深社会经济劣势，进一步增加失业、贫困和无家可归的风险，从而助长劣势的恶性循环。这些结果也可能与刑事司法系统内的侮辱性态度和后果有关。	Drug use disorders can also deepen socioeconomic disadvantage, further increasing the risk of unemployment, poverty and homelessness, thereby contributing to a vicious cycle of disadvantage. These results may also be related to stigmatizing attitudes and consequences within the criminal justice system.	no
妇女、少数民族和移民、性取向多样化群体、因武装冲突或灾难而流离失所的人以及农村环境中的人也可能受到吸毒病症的过重影响，或者在获得治疗服务方面遇到问题。	Women, ethnic minorities and immigrants, sexually diverse groups, people displaced by armed conflict or disasters, and people in rural settings may also be disproportionately affected by substance use disorders or experience problems accessing treatment services.	no
根据估计因残疾和过早死亡而损失的健康寿命年数的残疾调整寿命年（DALY)指标，在过去10年中，有害的吸毒对范围更广的社会影响加重。	The wider societal impact of harmful drug use has increased over the past 10 years, according to the disability-adjusted life-year (DALY) indicator, which estimates years of healthy life lost to disability and premature death.	no
2007年至2018年间，归因于吸毒的全球残疾调整寿命年数增加了 17%。	Global disability-adjusted life years attributable to drug use increased by 17% between 2007 and 2018.	no
注射吸毒者中常见的未经治疗的丙型肝炎导致的肝癌的相关残疾调整寿命年数增幅特别高——达到40%。	The increase in DALYs associated with liver cancer from untreated hepatitis C, which is common among injecting drug users, was particularly high - up to 40%.	no
毒品和暴力之间的关系错综复杂很难确定精神活性物质的使用和暴力之间的所有因果关系。	The relationship between drugs and violence is intricate and difficult to establish all causal relationships between psychoactive substance use and violence.	no
全球范围的有限数据表明，迷醉可能是杀人的一个重要因素。	Limited data worldwide suggest that intoxication may be an important factor in homicide.	no
但在暴力事件中，酒精的作用似乎比毒品更大。	But alcohol appears to play a bigger role than drugs in violent incidents.	no
虽然吸毒可能会导致犯罪，但在某些情况下，这种联系可以部分归因于多种中介因素，如社会经济劣势以及由个人风险、家庭环境和同龄人影响造成的其他类型的逆境。	While drug use may lead to crime, in some cases this association can be attributed in part to multiple mediating factors, such as socioeconomic disadvantage and other types of adversity resulting from personal risk, family environment, and peer influence.	no
贩毒和暴力之间的联系是多方面的。	The link between drug trafficking and violence is multifaceted.	no
如果已有稳定的犯罪结构，包括国际贩毒在内的大规模有组织犯罪活动有可能在无暴力的情况下实施。	Large-scale organized crime, including international drug trafficking, is likely to be carried out without violence if stable criminal structures are in place.	no
短期内，暴力的存在和程度与其说取决于贩运的数量，不如说取决于造成有组织犯罪集团之间力量平衡不稳定的某些变化，例如非法市场规模的变化，知名罪犯的死亡或监禁，以及使一个集团弱于另一个集团的执法措施。	In the short term, the presence and extent of violence depend less on the volume of trafficking than on certain changes that destabilize the balance of power among organized criminal groups, such as changes in the size of the illegal market, the death or incarceration of high-profile criminals, and enforcement measures that make one group weaker than another.	no
最新趋势	latest trends	yes
吸毒大麻是最常用的物质，类阿片危害最大	Marijuana is most commonly used substance, opioids most harmful	yes
据估计，2018年使用大麻的有 1.92 亿人，使之成为全球使用最多的毒品。	An estimated 192 million people used cannabis in 2018, making it the most used drug globally.	yes
相比之下，2018年使用类阿片的有5,800万人。	In comparison, 58 million people used opioids in 2018.	yes
但阿片类药物的相关危害却因使用者较少而受到忽视。	But the harms associated with opioids have been overlooked due to the low number of users.	yes
在2017年与吸毒病症有关的估计167,000例死亡中，有66%是这类物质造成的，在据信为吸毒导致的残疾或过早死亡而损失的2,100万年寿命中，有50%是这类物质造成的。	Substances were responsible for 66 percent of the estimated 167,000 deaths related to substance use disorders in 2017 and 50 percent of the 21 million years of life believed to be lost to drug-related disability or premature death.	yes
合成类阿片的非医疗使用加剧了公共卫生危机	Non-medical use of synthetic opioids exacerbates public health crisis	yes
在西非、中部非洲和北非，加剧类阿片危机的是曲马多；在北美则是芬太尼。这两个区域在经济、人口统计数据或一般吸毒模式方面几乎没有共同点，但都在奋力抗击由容易获得且生产成本低的物质助长的类阿片危机。	In West, Central and North Africa, it is tramadol that is fueling the opioid crisis; in North America it is fentanyl. The two regions, which have little in common in terms of economics, demographics or general drug use patterns, are struggling to combat an opioid crisis fueled by readily available and cheaply produced substances.	yes
在北美，芬太尼等合成类阿片的使用导致了20年来类阿片过量致死人数增加。	In North America, the use of synthetic opioids such as fentanyl has contributed to a 20-year increase in opioid overdose deaths.	yes
2018年，在美国登记的67,367例过量死亡中，有三分之二涉及芬太尼。	In 2018, two-thirds of the 67,367 overdose deaths registered in the United States involved fentanyl.	yes
加拿大也报告了类似的结果，只是数字较低。	Canada reported similar results, albeit with lower numbers.	no
芬太尼导致过量死亡的部分原因是非法药物市场上的芬太尼药效不可预测。	Part of the reason fentanyl is responsible for overdose deaths is the unpredictable potency of fentanyl in the illicit drug market.	no
在西非、中部非洲和北非，非医疗用途曲马多的市场已有大幅增长。	The market for non-medical use of tramadol has grown significantly in West, Central and North Africa.	no
在该区域，接受治疗的曲马多使用病症患者越来越多。	There is an increasing number of patients receiving treatment for tramadol use disorders in the region.	no
2017年，全球截获的曲马多数量显著增加，达到125吨以上的峰值。	The amount of tramadol intercepted globally increased significantly in 2017, peaking at more than 125 tons.	no
但2018年，在印度通过一项监管曲马多的新法律之后，全球缉获量降至32吨。	But in 2018, after India passed a new law regulating tramadol, global seizures fell to 32 tons.	no
促成这两地危机的是制造简单和生产成本低，此外还有对曲马多和许多芬太尼类似物或其前体缺乏国际监管。	Contributing to the crisis in both places is the simplicity and low cost of production, as well as the lack of international regulation of tramadol and many fentanyl analogs or their precursors.	no
使这两地危机恶化的是这些物质在药品市场和非法市场上都有供应，因而更加难以发现和防止其滥用。	Compounding the crisis in both places is the fact that these substances are available in both pharmaceutical and illicit markets, making their abuse even more difficult to detect and prevent.	no
兴奋剂使用不断增多	Doping use on the rise	no
兴奋剂领域以可卡因和甲基苯丙胺为主，这两种物质在其主要市场的使用量都在上升。	The stimulant sector is dominated by cocaine and methamphetamine, both of which are seeing rising use in their major markets.	no
2018年使用可卡因的约有1,900万人，因为可卡因在北美和西欧颇为流行。	About 19 million people used cocaine in 2018, as cocaine is prevalent in North America and Western Europe.	no
同年使用苯丙胺的约有2,700万人，其中甲基苯丙胺是东南亚和北美使用最多的苯丙胺类兴奋剂。	About 27 million people used amphetamines in the same year, with methamphetamine being the most used ATS in South-East Asia and North America.	no
根据所掌握的多数指标，20年来这两个区域甲基苯丙胺的使用一直在扩大。	According to most indicators available, methamphetamine use has been increasing in both regions for 20 years.	no
在一些市场上，可卡因和甲基苯丙胺可以共存，有时是相互替代，这样一种药物的使用量上升时另一种药物的使用量就下降，有时是同时增加和减少以满足同一市场的需求。	In some markets, cocaine and methamphetamine can co-exist, sometimes substituting for each other, so that use of one drug rises while the use of the other falls, sometimes both increasing and decreasing to meet demand in the same market.	no
新冠肺炎使注射吸毒者的风险增高	COVID-19 Puts Injecting Drug Users at Higher Risk	no
据估计，2018年注射吸毒的约有1,130万人，全球艾滋病毒感染约有10%是注射吸毒造成的。	An estimated 11.3 million people injected drugs in 2018, and about 10% of global HIV infections are attributable to injecting drug use.	no
注射吸毒者感染艾滋病毒的超过100万人，患丙型肝炎的有550万人。	More than 1 million people who inject drugs are infected with HIV and 5.5 million with hepatitis C.	no
2017年，因吸毒死亡的约有 58.5万人，其中一半死于丙型肝炎引起的肝病，而注射吸毒者的丙型肝炎大多仍未得到治疗。	Of the estimated 585,000 drug deaths in 2017, half were due to liver disease caused by hepatitis C, which remains largely untreated among people who inject drugs.	no
5 新冠肺炎限制措施造成的类阿片短缺可能导致使用者代之以酒精或苯二氮类药物等更容易获得的物质，或者将类阿片与合成药物混合。	5 Opioid shortages caused by COVID-19 restrictions may lead users to substitute for more readily available substances such as alcohol or benzodiazepines, or to mix opioids with synthetic drugs.	no
随着一些使用者改用注射或更频繁地注射，可能会出现更多有害的使用方式。	More harmful patterns of use may emerge as some users switch to injections or inject more frequently.	no

美国升级“芯片战”重创全球半导体产业-中新网	The United States escalates its "chip war" and hits the global semiconductor industry hard-Chinanews.com	yes
最近，美国对华“芯片战”大有升级之势——先是荷兰、日本两国在美国施压下，同意启动对华半导体制造设备出口的管制；后有外媒报道，美国政府正考虑切断美国供应商与华为公司之间的所有联系，禁止美国供应商向华为提供任何产品；拜登政府还准备公布一项行政命令，限制美国对敏感的中国科技行业的投资……2023年开年不久，美国在遏制中国半导体相关产业发展上就恶招不断。	Recently, the U.S. "chip war" against China has been escalating. First, under the pressure of the U.S., the Netherlands and Japan agreed to start controlling the export of semiconductor manufacturing equipment to China; later, foreign media reported that the U.S. government is considering cutting off all connections between U.S. suppliers and Huawei, prohibiting U.S. suppliers from supplying any products to Huawei; the Biden administration is also preparing to issue an executive order to restrict U.S. investment in the sensitive Chinese technology industry... 2023 will soon begin, the U.S. has continued to make evil moves to curb the development of China's semiconductor-related industries.	yes
近年来，美国打击中国“芯”发展的动作从未停歇，一边精准打压对华半导体产供链，一边构建“去中国化”的半导体产业链联盟，图谋在先进半导体产业上彻底“甩开”中国。	In recent years, the United States has never stopped cracking down on the development of China's "chips." While precisely suppressing the semiconductor production and supply chain to China, it is building a "de-Sinicization" semiconductor industry chain alliance in an attempt to completely "get rid of" China in the advanced semiconductor industry.	yes
无论是拉拢韩国建立“技术同盟”，还是与韩国、日本和中国台湾地区建立芯片“四方联盟”，亦或借由美日印澳“四边机制”“印太经济框架”等机制建立半导体产业链“小圈子”，美国通过把政治化、阵营化、武器化的手段引入半导体产业，企图搭建美国主导的封闭产供链循环，从而弥补其在芯片制造领域的短板，维护其在全球芯片产业的优势地位。	Whether it is to win over South Korea to establish a "technical alliance," or to establish a chip "four-party alliance" with South Korea, Japan and Taiwan, or to establish a semiconductor industry chain through mechanisms such as the "four-party mechanism" of the United States, Japan, India and Australia, and the "Indo-Pacific Economic Framework," the United States has introduced the semiconductor industry by means of politicization, blocization, and weaponization, in an attempt to build a closed production and supply chain led by the United States, so as to make up for its shortcomings in the field of chip manufacturing and maintain its dominant position in the global chip industry.	yes
然而，美国大张旗鼓的对华“芯战术”，也是“伤敌一千自损八百”。	However, the US's "core tactics" against China with great fanfare is also "injury to the enemy by one thousand and self-injury to eight hundred."	yes

2月10日，中国理财网发布首批个人养老金理财产品名单，工银理财、农银理财和中邮理财的7只个人养老金理财产品正式发售。	On February 10, China Finance Network released the list of the first batch of personal pension wealth management products. Seven personal pension wealth management products from ICBC Wealth Management, Agricultural Bank of China Wealth Management and China Post Wealth Management were officially launched.	yes
至此，个人养老金账户的“货架”终于集齐个人养老金储蓄、个人养老金理财、个人养老金保险、个人养老金公募基金四类产品。	So far, the "shelves" of personal pension accounts have finally collected four types of products: personal pension savings, personal pension wealth management, personal pension insurance, and personal pension public funds.	yes
据介绍，首批个人养老金理财产品，全部为公募类净值型开放式产品，其中新发产品5只、存续产品2只，除1只产品为混合类产品外，其余6只产品均为固定收益类产品。	According to reports, the first batch of personal pension wealth management products are all open-ended public offering net worth products, including 5 new products and 2 existing products. Except for 1 product that is a mixed product, the remaining 6 products are fixed income products.	yes
北京青年报记者看到，5只新发产品中有4只来自工银理财，全部是固定收益类产品，最短持有期限分别为365天、540天、720天和1080天，对应的业绩比较基准(年化)分别为3.70 % - 4.20 % 、 4.10 % - 4.60 % 、 4.40 % - 4.90 % 、 5.25 % - 5.75 % 。	A reporter from Beijing Youth Daily saw that 4 of the 5 new products came from ICBC Wealth Management, all of which were fixed-income products, and the minimum holding periods were 365 days, 540 days, 720 days and 1080 days. The corresponding performance benchmarks (annualized) were 3.70%-4.20%, 4.10%-4.60%, 4.40%-4.90%, 5.25%-5.75%.	yes
剩余一只新发产品是“邮银财富添颐·鸿锦最短持有1095 天 1 号 ” ， 也是固定收益类产品，2月10日开始募集，2月19日结束募集，风险等级为二级。	The remaining one newly released product is "Post Bank Fortune Tianyi · Hongjin Shortest Holding 1095 Days No. 1," which is also a fixed-income product. The fundraising started on February 10 and ended on February 19. The risk level is Level 2.	yes

首批个人养老金理财产品发售，标志着个人养老金投资者可正式通过个人养老金资金账户购买理财产品。	The launch of the first batch of personal pension wealth management products marks that individual pension investors can officially purchase wealth management products through personal pension fund accounts.	no
去年11月银保监会制定了《商业银行和理财公司个人养老金业务管理暂行办法 》 。	In November last year, the China Banking and Insurance Regulatory Commission formulated the "Interim Measures for the Administration of Personal Pension Business of Commercial Banks and Wealth Management Companies."	no
《办法》规定，参加人可以通过个人养老金资金账户购买个人养老储蓄、个人养老金理财产品、个人养老金保险产品、个人养老金公募基金产品等个人养老金产品。	The "Measures" stipulate that participants can purchase personal pension savings, personal pension wealth management products, personal pension insurance products, personal pension public offering fund products and other personal pension products through their personal pension fund accounts.	no
随后，人社部、财政部、国家税务总局三部门发布通知，明确个人养老金制度在北京、天津，以及河北石家庄、雄安新区，山西晋城市等36个先行城市和地区启动实施。	Subsequently, the Ministry of Human Resources and Social Security, the Ministry of Finance, and the State Administration of Taxation issued a notice specifying that the personal pension system will be implemented in 36 leading cities and regions including Beijing, Tianjin, Shijiazhuang in Hebei, Xiongan New District, and Jincheng in Shanxi.	no
截至2022年底，个人养老金参加人数1954万人，缴费人数613万人，总缴费金额142亿元。	By the end of 2022, the number of individual pension participants will be 19.54 million, the number of contributors will be 6.13 million, and the total payment amount will be 14.2 billion yuan.	no
此前，参与试点的银行只上架了个人养老储蓄、个人养老金保险产品和个人养老金公募基金三类产品。	Previously, the banks participating in the pilot had only listed three types of products: personal pension savings, personal pension insurance products and personal pension public offering funds.	no
如今，个人养老金理财产品也聚齐之后，投资者该如何选择？	Now that personal pension wealth management products are also available, how should investors choose?	no
交银理财产品研发部专家表示，相比其他个人养老金产品，试点阶段的养老理财产品和个人养老金理财产品均具有三方面的特点。	Experts from the R&D Department of Bank of Communications Wealth Management Products said that compared with other personal pension products, the pension wealth management products in the pilot phase and personal pension wealth management products have three characteristics.	no
一是稳健性，风险管理机制更加健全，投资策略和理念更为稳健，并实施非母行第三方独立托管。	The first is robustness. The risk management mechanism is more complete, the investment strategy and philosophy are more stable, and the third-party independent custody of the non-parent bank is implemented.	no
二是长期性，试点阶段养老理财产品的期限都在5年及以上，下一步发行的个人养老金理财产品，最短持有期原则上为1年，鼓励持有3年以上。	The second is long-term. The term of pension wealth management products in the pilot phase is 5 years or more. The personal pension wealth management products issued in the next step have a minimum holding period of 1 year in principle, and are encouraged to hold more than 3 years.	no
三是普惠性，产品购买门槛低，起购点一般为1元，有的低至0.01元，产品的托管费、管理费等费率更加优惠。	The third is inclusiveness. The product purchase threshold is low. The minimum purchase point is generally 1 yuan, and some are as low as 0.01 yuan. The product custody fee, management fee and other rates are more favorable.	no
专业人士指出，投资者要根据产品特点和自己的风险承受能力进行选择。	Professionals pointed out that investors should make choices based on product characteristics and their own risk tolerance.	no
个人养老金储蓄具有期限较长、利率较高、安全性高的特点，适合风险承受能力弱的人群；个人养老金保险产品重在保障，比较适合无法承担投资风险，可以接受稳定收益的人群；而个人养老金理财产品和公募基金产品不保本也不保收益，有一定投资风险，但预期收益较高，适合具备一定的金融知识、风险承担能力较高的人群。	Personal pension savings have the characteristics of long term, high interest rate, and high security, which are suitable for people with weak risk tolerance; personal pension insurance products focus on protection, and are more suitable for people who cannot bear investment risks but can accept stable returns; however, personal pension wealth management products and public offering fund products do not guarantee capital or income, and have certain investment risks, but the expected returns are relatively high, and they are suitable for people with certain financial knowledge and high risk-taking ability.	no

健身行业应摆脱信任危机-中新网	The fitness industry should get rid of the crisis of trust-Chinanews.com	yes
又一大型健身房“暴雷”？	Another large gym "thunderstorm"?	yes
近日，知名健身机构中健健身会员维权问题引起社会关注。	Recently, the well-known fitness organization Zhongjian Fitness members' rights protection issues have attracted social attention.	yes
春节后不少会员发现自己所在门店没有正常营业，随后，关于该机构倒闭跑路的传闻引起会员恐慌，导致公安、人社部门介入。	After the Spring Festival, many members found that their stores were not operating normally. Later, rumors about the organization's closure and escape caused panic among members, which led to the intervention of the public security and human resources and social security departments.	yes
最后，该机构相关负责人出面回应，承诺会努力保障好员工和会员的合法权益，风波才得以平息。	In the end, the relevant person in charge of the organization came forward to respond, promising to work hard to protect the legitimate rights and interests of employees and members, and the turmoil subsided.	yes
个别健身机构的部分门店出现经营问题，暂时关闭，消费者本可心平气和等待问题解决，为何不少会员的第一反应是“大事不妙”？	Some stores of individual fitness institutions have business problems and are temporarily closed. Consumers can calmly wait for the problem to be resolved. Why do many members' first reaction is "something is not good"?	yes
健身俱乐部会员维权风波背后，是行业信任危机的深层次问题。	Behind the turmoil of fitness club members' rights protection is the deep-seated problem of the industry's trust crisis.	yes
国内传统健身房普遍采取预付费模式，“赚用户不来的钱”是其发展的底层逻辑。	Traditional domestic gyms generally adopt a prepaid model, and "earning money that users can't come" is the underlying logic of their development.	yes
通过预售会员卡获取现金流，不断开新店，看似能够循环往复，实则寅吃卯粮，无法形成稳定的盈利模式。	Obtaining cash flow through the pre-sale of membership cards and constantly opening new stores seems to be able to repeat itself, but in fact, it is impossible to form a stable profit model.	yes
健身房跑路等行业负面信息频频传出，对消费者信心造成强烈冲击。	Negative information about industries such as running in the gym frequently spreads, which has a strong impact on consumer confidence.	yes
从市场前景看，健身房当然算得上是一门有“钱途”的好生意。	From the perspective of market prospects, gyms can of course be regarded as a good business with "money prospects."	no
健身赛道虽然起起伏伏，但始终受到资本关注。	Although the fitness track has ups and downs, it has always attracted the attention of capital.	no
多项数据显示，文体消费等领域热度不断攀升，市场持续回暖。	A number of data show that the popularity of cultural and sports consumption and other fields continues to rise, and the market continues to pick up.	no
具体到健身市场，随着居民生活水平稳步提高，健康生活理念深入人心，健身行业发展大有可为。	Specific to the fitness market, with the steady improvement of residents' living standards and the concept of healthy living deeply rooted in the hearts of the people, the fitness industry has great potential for development.	no
形势越是趋好，行业越需重视发展质量。	The better the situation is, the more the industry needs to pay attention to the quality of development.	no
然而，个别机构对消费复苏后的健身市场盲目乐观，刚从危机中走出来，又吹响开疆拓土的号角，把融资资金一股脑投入新店建设上。	However, some institutions are blindly optimistic about the fitness market after the recovery of consumption. Just after coming out of the crisis, they sounded the clarion call to expand the territory and invested all the financing funds into the construction of new stores.	no
不可否认，这几年受疫情影响，不少机构退出，行业重新洗牌，有实力的企业此时选择性地加大收购力度、重新布局，未尝不是新机遇。	It is undeniable that due to the impact of the epidemic in the past few years, many institutions have withdrawn and the industry has been reshuffled. At this time, powerful companies are selectively increasing their acquisitions and reorganizing their layout. This may not be a new opportunity.	no
但是，健身市场发展要想进入良性循环，迈上行稳致远的康庄大道，行业就必须改变传统模式，改变经营策略。	However, if the development of the fitness market wants to enter a virtuous circle and take a steady and long-term path, the industry must change the traditional model and change its business strategy.	no
只有稳扎稳打，重新建立起消费者的信任度、安全感，才能真正赢得市场、赢得未来。	Only by working steadily and re-establishing the trust and sense of security of consumers can we truly win the market and win the future.	no
相比大建新店抢占市场，健身行业当前更需要的是沉下心来优化服务，用高质量发展来稳住用户。	Compared with building new stores to seize the market, what the fitness industry needs now is to settle down to optimize services and stabilize users with high-quality development.	no
首先，要靠服务留住用户。	First of all, it is necessary to rely on services to retain users.	no
健身房属于服务行业，其本质是坚持“用户导向”，要紧紧围绕用户需求，把经营重心放在服务提质升级上。	Gyms belong to the service industry, and its essence is to adhere to the "user orientation," closely focus on user needs, and focus on improving service quality and upgrading.	no
其次，要靠数字化转型提升用户体验。	Second, rely on digital transformation to improve user experience.	no
比如当下流行的互联网健身房模式，实现用户按次付费和场地自选。	For example, the current popular Internet gym model enables users to pay per view and choose venues on their own.	no
同时，身体数据、运动数据得以有效利用，还可以满足社交需求，实现从线上到线下完整的服务闭环。	At the same time, body data and sports data can be effectively used to meet social needs and realize a complete closed-loop service from online to offline.	no
没有私教推销，没有巨额年卡，用户对健身机构“跑路”的担忧降低了，信任感也就提升了。	There is no personal training promotion, no huge annual card, users are less worried about "running away" from fitness institutions, and their sense of trust is also improved.	no
另外，还要积极探索多元业态。	In addition, we should actively explore diversified business forms.	no
如今，体育消费已经从单一服务走向场景消费，健身俱乐部有望成为消费新入口，围绕健身所需的运动补给和健身器械等周边产品或将成为新的盈利点，为消费者提供更丰富选择。	Today, sports consumption has shifted from a single service to scene consumption. Fitness clubs are expected to become a new entry point for consumption. Peripheral products such as sports supplies and fitness equipment for fitness may become new profit points, providing consumers with more choices.	no
姜天骄	Jiang Tianjiao	no
买贵退差价！	Buy expensive refund price difference!	yes
南京楼市再现“差价赔付”-中新网	Nanjing property market reappears "payment for price difference"-Chinanews.com	yes
扬子晚报讯(记者 马祚波)扬子晚报/紫牛新闻记者10日在采访中发现，十余年未见的“保价协议”又重回了南京楼市，位于江北新区的一家楼盘宣称“差价赔付”，在交房前其他房源的优惠大于之前的折扣，开发商愿意为买房人换房并退还差价。	Yangzi Evening News (Reporter Ma Zuobo) Yangzi Evening News/Ziniu News reporter found in an interview on the 10th that the "price protection agreement" that had not been seen for more than ten years has returned to the Nanjing property market. Before the house is handed over, the discount of other housing sources is greater than the previous discount, and the developer is willing to change the house for the buyer and refund the difference.	yes
“保价协议”条件可不少	There are many conditions for the "guaranteed price agreement"	yes
这家位于江北新区的楼盘名为保利扬子萃云台，看房人孙先生告诉记者，他在上周末逛楼盘时发现了一则“声明”。	This real estate located in Jiangbei New District is called Poly Yangzi Cuiyun Terrace. Mr. Sun, the viewer, told reporters that he found a "statement" when he was shopping for real estate last weekend.	yes
他发给记者的图片上显示，该楼盘的开发商承诺，凡是在2月1日-2月28日期间购买房源的，自双方签订买卖合同之日起至对应房源交付，若该项目其他房源的优惠折扣大于之前购房所享折扣的(限与该商品房属于同一户型、同一楼栋、同一单元、同一物业类型的其他未售商品房)，开发商可以为购房者换房并退还差价。	The picture he sent to the reporter shows that the developer of the real estate promises that anyone who purchases a house between February 1 and February 28 will start from the date when the two parties sign the sales contract until the corresponding house is delivered. If the preferential discount of other houses is greater than the discount enjoyed by the previous house purchase (limited to other unsold commercial houses of the same type, same building, same unit, and same property type as the commercial house), the developer can change the house for the buyer and refund the difference.	yes
孙先生表示，置业顾问表示这其实就是一份“保价协议”，目的是让买家放心出手，不用担心开发企业降价促销，“现在就怕买完了它就降价了，去售楼处闹吧没时间，不闹的话也确实窝心”。	Mr. Sun said that the real estate consultant said that this is actually a "price protection agreement," the purpose is to let buyers feel at ease and don't have to worry about the price reduction of the development company. "Now I'm afraid that the price will be reduced after buying it. Go to the sales office to make trouble. No time, if you don't make trouble, it's really heartwarming."	yes
还有不少买房人则认为，“保价协议”虽然是在给购房者吃“定心丸”，不过条件却不低。	There are still many house buyers who believe that although the "price protection agreement" is to give house buyers "reassurance," the conditions are not low.	yes
打算在江北买一套刚需房的郑女士说，保价的房源首先是要同一户型，还得在同一楼栋、同一个单元，买家可以比价的房源寥寥，因此“门槛”还是蛮高的。	Ms. Zheng, who intends to buy a new house in Jiangbei, said that the price-insured house must first be of the same type, and must be in the same building and the same unit. There are very few houses that buyers can compare prices, so the "threshold" is still quite high.	yes
也有购房者认为，由于信息不对称，销售时不排除给出额外的让利，买家“维权”的难度不小。	There are also buyers who believe that due to information asymmetry, it is not ruled out that additional concessions will be given during the sale, and it is not easy for buyers to "protect their rights."	yes
能否留住买房人有待观察	Whether it can keep house buyers remains to be seen	no
记者在南京网上房地产上查询得知，该楼盘于去年11月首领两幢楼共计252套房源的销许，户型面积有105平方米、114平方米、129平方米等，全装修销许均价为39843元/㎡。	The reporter inquired on the real estate online in Nanjing and learned that the real estate sold a total of 252 suites in two buildings in November last year. The price is 39843 yuan/m2.	no
不过两个多月过去，网上房地产显示目前该楼盘的未售总套数为157套，占比为62.3%，其中8号楼共计128套，未售套数达113套，7号楼的124套中也有44套未售，项目的总成交套数只有33套，占比仅为13%。	However, more than two months later, online real estate shows that the total number of unsold units in this building is 157, accounting for 62.3%. There are also 44 unsold sets, and the total number of transactions of the project is only 33 sets, accounting for only 13%.	no
市场人士介绍，“保价协议”在2008年也曾在南京出现过。	According to market sources, the "guaranteed price agreement" also appeared in Nanjing in 2008.	no
当年8月份，河西黄山路上的楼盘横塘西苑为了吸引买房人眼球，推出了《保价计划》，具体内容为“公司郑重承诺，若一年内项目优惠幅度扩大，由此产生的差额，公司将按差额退还给老业主”。	In August of that year, Hengtang Xiyuan, a real estate project on Huangshan Road in Hexi, launched the "Price Guarantee Plan" in order to attract the attention of house buyers. The specific content was "The company solemnly promises that if the preferential margin of the project is expanded within a year, the difference will be refunded to the old owner."	no
此后2011年4月，南京也有9家楼盘拿出部分房源承诺“差价赔付”。	Afterwards, in April 2011, 9 real estate properties in Nanjing took out part of their listings and promised to "compensate for the price difference."	no
“楼市在回暖，此时更需要一针‘强心剂’。	"The property market is picking up, and at this time we need a shot of'heart booster'.	no
”南京地产行业一位资深操盘手沈先生表示，“保价协议”也是房企的营销方式之一。	"Mr. Shen, a senior trader in the Nanjing real estate industry, said that the "price protection agreement" is also one of the marketing methods of real estate companies.	no
他认为如今开发企业比买房人更需要信心，推出“保价协议”其实也是在给其打气。	He believes that development companies need more confidence than house buyers nowadays, and the launch of the "price protection agreement" is actually to encourage them.	no
至于能否留住买房人，他表示这取决于调控政策、贷款门槛等多重因素的影响，就目前来看仍有待观察。	As for whether the buyers can be retained, he said that it depends on the impact of multiple factors such as regulatory policies and loan thresholds, and it remains to be seen at present.	no
多项数据衰退 台湾经济开年表现不佳-中新网	A number of data recession, Taiwan's economy performed poorly in the beginning of the year - Chinanews.com	yes
新华社台北2月11日电(记者赵博、黄扬)出口贸易额“连五黑”，制造业采购经理人指数(PMI)连续7个月紧缩，消费者物价指数(CPI)又见“3字头”……近期，台湾当局陆续发布2023年1月经济数据。	Xinhua News Agency, Taipei, February 11 (reporters Zhao Bo and Huang Yang) The export trade volume is "five blacks in a row," the manufacturing purchasing managers index (PMI) has shrunk for seven consecutive months, and the consumer price index (CPI) has seen "3 prefix..."Recently, the Taiwan authorities have successively released economic data for January 2023.	yes
专家分析认为，台湾经济开年表现欠佳，增长压力不小。	According to expert analysis, Taiwan's economy performed poorly at the beginning of the year, and the growth pressure is not small.	yes
据台当局财政事务主管部门公布，台湾地区今年1月出口315.1亿美元，年减21.2%，连续第5个月负增长。	According to the financial affairs department of the Taiwan authorities, Taiwan's exports in January this year were 31.51 billion US dollars, an annual decrease of 21.2%, and it was the fifth consecutive month of negative growth.	yes
11项主要出口货类的出口额与去年同期相比，均出现衰退。	Compared with the same period last year, the export value of 11 major export categories all declined.	yes
塑橡胶及其制品、光学器材跌幅最深，分别年减37.6%、35.7%。	Plastic rubber and its products, optical equipment fell the most, with an annual decrease of 37.6% and 35.7% respectively.	yes
电子零组件出口年减20.1%，创11年来最大减幅。	Exports of electronic components and components fell by 20.1% year-on-year, the largest decline in 11 years.	yes
其中，集成电路年减18.3%，创14年来最大跌势。	Among them, integrated circuits decreased by 18.3% year-on-year, the largest decline in 14 years.	yes
该部门统计处长蔡美娜表示，这显示消费性电子产业需求疲弱效应扩散，电子产业进入修正期。	Cai Meina, head of the statistics department of the department, said that this shows that the weak demand effect of the consumer electronics industry has spread, and the electronics industry has entered a correction period.	yes
统计显示，1月台湾地区进出口双降，出超金额仅23.4亿美元，创近3年来最低水平。	Statistics show that Taiwan's imports and exports both fell in January, and the excess amount was only US$2.34 billion, the lowest level in nearly three years.	yes
台当局财政事务主管部门认为，全球终端需求减少，产业调整库存抑制厂商购料意愿，出口颓势短期难见改善，台湾今年首季出口衰退恐高于预期。	The financial affairs department of the Taiwan authorities believes that the decline in global end-use demand and the adjustment of industrial inventories have restrained manufacturers' willingness to purchase materials. The decline in exports will hardly improve in the short term. Taiwan's export decline in the first quarter of this year may be higher than expected.	no
据台湾中华经济研究院发布，今年1月台湾制造业采购经理人指数(PMI)经季节调整后为40.4%，较去年12月续跌3.3个百分点，连续7个月紧缩。	According to Taiwan's Zhonghua Economic Research Institute, Taiwan's Manufacturing Purchasing Managers' Index (PMI) in January this year was 40.4% after seasonal adjustment, down 3.3 percentage points from December last year, and contracted for seven consecutive months.	no
经济监测指标体系中，PMI以50%为荣枯线，指数大于50%，代表景气扩张，反之为紧缩。	In the economic monitoring index system, PMI takes 50% as the line of prosperity and decline, and an index greater than 50% means that the economy is expanding, and vice versa is contraction.	no
1月台湾PMI五项组成指标中，新增订单、生产与人力雇佣紧缩，供应商交货时间下降，存货紧缩。	Among the five components of Taiwan's PMI in January, new orders, production and manpower employment tightened, suppliers' delivery times decreased, and inventories tightened.	no
六大产业全数回报PMI紧缩，各产业依紧缩速度排序为电力暨机械设备产业(35.1%)、电子暨光学产业(35.2%)、化学暨生技医疗产业(39.2%)、基础原物料产业(42.4%)、交通工具产业(42.6%)与食品暨纺织产业(45.7%)。	The six major industries all reported PMI contraction, and the industries were ranked according to the speed of contraction as electric power and mechanical equipment industry (35.1%), electronics and optical industry (35.2%), chemical and biotechnology medical industry (39.2%), basic raw material industry (42.4%), transportation industry (42.6%) and food and textile industry (45.7%).	no
物价方面，台当局“主计总处”公布，今年1月台湾CPI年增率为3.04%，自去年7月以来再度冲破3%。	In terms of prices, Taiwan's "General Office of Accounting and Accounting" announced that in January this year, the annual growth rate of Taiwan's CPI was 3.04%, breaking through 3% again since July last year.	no
其中，蔬菜价格飞涨28.25%，创17个月新高。	Among them, vegetable prices soared 28.25%, hitting a 17-month high.	no
台“主计总处”专门委员曹志弘坦言，菜价涨幅确实超乎预期，排除春节因素，今年1月和2月平均CPI应接近去年12月的2.71%，通胀压力还是存在，且仍在高点。	Cao Zhihong, a special committee member of Taiwan's "General Office of Accounting and Accounting," said frankly that the increase in vegetable prices has indeed exceeded expectations. Excluding the Spring Festival factor, the average CPI in January and February this year should be close to 2.71% in December last year. Inflationary pressure still exists and is still high.	no
展望今年台湾经济，综合《联合报》、“Yahoo财经”等岛内媒体报道，专家表示悲观。	Looking forward to Taiwan's economy this year, experts expressed pessimism based on the reports of Taiwan's media such as "United Daily News" and "Yahoo Finance."	no
台“中央大学”经济系教授吴大任分析，出口衰退可能造成出口制造业厂商现金流出现问题，债务违约风险上升。	Wu Daren, a professor of economics at Taiwan's "Central University," analyzed that the decline in exports may cause cash flow problems for export manufacturing companies and increase the risk of debt default.	no
同时，订单减少导致厂商削减人力成本，影响劳动市场和家庭经济，反过来冲击消费能力。	At the same time, the reduction in orders leads manufacturers to cut labor costs, which affects the labor market and the household economy, which in turn impacts consumption capacity.	no
台湾经济研究院研究员邱达生认为，今年欧美通胀状况未解，需求持续萎缩，预估台湾出口衰退会延续到上半年。	Qiu Dasheng, a researcher at the Taiwan Institute of Economic Research, believes that the inflation situation in Europe and the United States is still unresolved this year, and demand continues to shrink. It is estimated that the decline in Taiwan's exports will continue into the first half of the year.	no
由于台湾经济靠出口支撑，受出口低迷影响，全年经济增长表现将不如去年。	Since Taiwan's economy is supported by exports, affected by the sluggish exports, the annual economic growth performance will not be as good as last year.	no
“全球复苏的重要引擎”-中新网	"An important engine for global recovery"-Chinanews.com	yes
“应对新冠疫情冲击，中国经济展现出了强大韧性。	"In response to the impact of the COVID-19 pandemic, the Chinese economy has shown strong resilience.	yes
近期市场预期表明，国际社会普遍看好中国未来发展。	Recent market expectations show that the international community is generally optimistic about China's future development.	yes
”西班牙知名中国问题专家、中国政策观察网名誉顾问胡里奥·里奥斯日前接受本报记者采访时表示，当前中国疫情防控进入新阶段，经济社会发展活力将进一步得到释放。	"Julio Rios, a well-known Spanish expert on China and honorary consultant of China Policy Observation Network, said in an interview with our reporter that the current epidemic prevention and control in China has entered a new stage, and the vitality of economic and social development will be further released.	yes
里奥斯表示，面对各种超预期因素冲击，中国以非凡的经济治理经验和措施沉着应对，充分体现出其经济韧性和管理水平。	Rios said that in the face of various shocks beyond expectations, China responded calmly with extraordinary economic governance experience and measures, which fully demonstrated its economic resilience and management level.	yes
中国坚定不移扩大对外开放的同时，经济发展的内生动力不断增强，国有企业和民营企业协同发展。	While China is unswervingly expanding its opening up to the outside world, the endogenous driving force of economic development has been continuously strengthened, and state-owned enterprises and private enterprises have developed in coordination.	yes

与2021年相比，2022年应届留学生规模同比增长8.6%，回国求职留学生数量再创新高。	Compared with 2021, the number of international students graduating in 2022 will increase by 8.6% year-on-year, and the number of international students returning to China for job hunting will hit a new high.	yes

种植牙齿指的是一种以植入骨组织内的下部结构为基础来支持、固位上部牙修复体的缺牙修复方式。	Dental implant refers to a method of restoring missing teeth based on the underlying structure of bone implant tissue to support and retain the upper tooth restoration.	yes
记者从郑州大学第一附属医院了解到，以单颗常规种植为例，从种植到最后修复，价格大概要一万六七千元左右。	The reporter learned from the First Affiliated Hospital of Zhengzhou University that taking a single conventional planting as an example, the price from planting to final restoration is about 16,000 to 7,000 yuan.	yes
