近年来，既有刘畊宏、东方甄选等现象级大V，也有在垂直细分领域出现的不少非大众所知的达人和商家，他们通过持续打造符合自己品牌调性的优质内容，提升长期经营效益。	In recent years, there have been phenomenon-level big Vs such as Liu Genghong and Dongfang Selection, as well as many unknown talents and merchants in the vertical segment. They continue to create high-quality content that matches their own brand tonality, and improve the long-term business benefits.	no
抖音电商明星作者运营负责人高亚轩介绍，过去一年有627万创作者通过抖音电商将内容变现，他们的内容创作量增长了252%，总成交额也翻了一倍以上。	According to Gao Yaxuan, head of Douyin e-commerce star author operations, 6.27 million creators have monetized content through Douyin e-commerce in the past year. Their content creation volume has increased by 252%, and their total turnover has more than doubled.	no
“在这些数字背后，我们能感受到一个蓬勃生长、具有旺盛生命力的作者生态。	"Behind these figures, we can feel a thriving and vigorous author ecology.	no
”高亚轩说。	"Gao Yaxuan said.	no
北京师范大学传播创新与未来媒体实验平台此前发布了《电商行业内容生态健康指数(ECHI)报告》，从数据维度解析了当前电商行业中“新变量”——优质内容的重要性，运用指数对国内27家主流电商平台内容生态情况进行了评估。	The Communication Innovation and Future Media Experiment Platform of Beijing Normal University previously released the "E-commerce Industry Content Ecological Health Index (ECHI) Report," which analyzed the "new variable" in the current e-commerce industry from the data dimension - the importance of high-quality content, and used the index to evaluate the content ecology of 27 domestic mainstream e-commerce platforms.	no
根据上述报告的电商行业内容生态健康指数排名，抖音电商、快手、淘宝、拼多多、京东位居前五。	According to the ranking of the content ecological health index of the e-commerce industry in the above report, Douyin E-commerce, Kuaishou, Taobao, Pinduoduo, and JD.com rank in the top five.	no
报告认为，电商行业内容生态是一个综合性概念，是将电商与内容进行整合，但并非所有内容都可与电商整合，好的PGC(专业生产内容)与UGC(用户原创内容)才是与电商进行整合的优质载体，内容平台价值越高，消费与推广的场景也就越来越丰富，电商植入的可能性也就越高，商业价值也就越强，这种公共领域和私人领域逐步集成分布的电商内容生产和内容消费的比例也就会越高。	The report believes that the content ecology of the e-commerce industry is a comprehensive concept that integrates e-commerce and content, but not all content can be integrated with e-commerce. Good PGC (professional production content) and UGC (user-generated content) are high-quality carriers for integration with e-commerce. The higher the value of the content platform, the more abundant the consumption and promotion scenarios, the higher the possibility of e-commerce implantation, and the stronger the commercial value. The proportion of e-commerce content production and content consumption will be higher as the public and private domains are gradually integrated and distributed.	no
现场，北京师范大学新闻传播学院教授、中国传媒经济与管理专业委员会理事长喻国明对《报告》做了分析解读。	At the scene, Yu Guoming, a professor at the School of Journalism and Communication of Beijing Normal University and chairman of the China Media Economics and Management Professional Committee, made an analysis and interpretation of the Report.	no
他表示，就内容价值而言，当前电商行业已经从“消费可及性”过渡到“消费品质化”阶段，优质、专业、差异化的内容是电商行业的“硬通货”。	He said that in terms of content value, the current e-commerce industry has transitioned from "consumption accessibility" to "consumption quality," and high-quality, professional, and differentiated content is the "hard currency" of the e-commerce industry.	no
同时，内容成为电商发展新阶段的根本和抓手，知识付费、专业性知识、KOL(关键意见领袖)等PGC内容开始在电商直播中成为标配。	At the same time, content has become the foundation and starting point of the new stage of e-commerce development, and PGC content such as knowledge payment, professional knowledge, and KOL (Key Opinion Leader) has begun to become standard in e-commerce live broadcasts.	no
展望电商行业的未来发展，喻国明提出两方面的建议。	Looking forward to the future development of the e-commerce industry, Yu Guoming put forward two suggestions.	no
一个是从内容结构提升的角度看，推动电商内容生态健康程度和质量整体提升，打造正向内容创作和管理标准，实现电商行业内容生态健康系统指数与动态均衡。	One is to promote the overall improvement of the ecological health and quality of e-commerce content from the perspective of content structure improvement, create positive content creation and management standards, and realize the index and dynamic balance of the e-commerce industry content ecological health system.	no
另一个是从外部生态看，要实现内容电商行业的健康发展和外部环境的价值协同与共创。	The other is from the perspective of external ecology, it is necessary to realize the healthy development of the content e-commerce industry and the value synergy and co-creation of the external environment.	no
“未来电商行业还需要更多的数据、人工智能方面的支持，形成对未来发展稳定性的预测；此外，为商家提供更规范、健康的成长空间，实现电商行业中企业、用户、产品与服务的价值协同，共创健康内容生态。	"In the future, the e-commerce industry will need more data and artificial intelligence support to form a prediction on the stability of future development; in addition, it will provide businesses with a more standardized and healthy growth space, and realize the value synergy of enterprises, users, and products in the e-commerce industry to create a healthy content ecosystem.	no
”(完)	"(over)	no
北交所融资融券交易业务下周启动-中新网	Margin trading and securities lending business of Beijing Stock Exchange will start next week-Chinanews.com	yes
本报讯(记者 孙杰)昨晚，北交所发布消息，经中国证监会批准，北京证券交易所融资融券交易业务将于2月13日正式启动，届时已取得北交所融资融券交易权限的证券公司可接受投资者委托，向北交所进行融资融券交易申报。	News from our newspaper (Reporter Sun Jie) Last night, the Beijing Stock Exchange announced that, with the approval of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, the Beijing Stock Exchange's margin financing and securities lending business will be officially launched on February 13. Securities companies with trading authority can accept the entrustment of investors to declare margin financing and securities lending transactions to CBEX.	yes
首批56只融资融券标的股票名单以2023年1月31日为计算基准日确定。	The list of the first batch of 56 stocks subject to margin financing and securities lending will be determined with January 31, 2023 as the calculation base date.	yes
北交所表示，融资融券标的股票名单和可充抵保证金证券名单将通过北交所官网的“信息披露-融资融券信息”栏目公布，方便投资者查询。	The CBEX stated that the list of stocks subject to margin financing and securities lending and the list of securities that can be used as margin will be published through the "Information Disclosure-Margin and Securities Lending Information" column of the CBEX's official website, which is convenient for investors to inquire.	yes
融资融券是证券市场重要的基础性制度，也是国际证券市场中较为成熟的交易方式。	Margin financing and securities lending is an important basic system in the securities market, and it is also a relatively mature trading method in the international securities market.	yes
去年9月2日，在宣布设立一周年之际，北交所对融资融券业务公开征求意见。	On September 2 last year, on the occasion of announcing the first anniversary of its establishment, the Beijing Stock Exchange publicly solicited opinions on the margin financing and securities lending business.	yes
北交所融资融券交易的启动是持续推进北交所市场制度建设、完善交易机制、提升二级市场定价功能的重要举措。	The launch of the CBEX's margin trading and securities lending transaction is an important measure to continue to promote the construction of the CBEX's market system, improve the trading mechanism, and enhance the pricing function of the secondary market.	yes
融资融券制度有利于丰富投资者交易策略，满足投资者多元交易需求，促进市场价格发现，进一步提升市场流动性。	The margin financing and securities lending system is conducive to enriching investors' trading strategies, meeting investors' diversified trading needs, promoting market price discovery, and further enhancing market liquidity.	yes
下一步，北交所将在中国证监会的领导下，持续做好融资融券业务各项保障工作，以投资者需求为导向丰富交易制度工具，完善相关配套机制，着力打造服务创新型中小企业的一流交易所。	In the next step, under the leadership of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, the CBEX will continue to do a good job in various guarantees for the margin financing and securities lending business, enrich the trading system tools based on investor needs, improve relevant supporting mechanisms, and strive to create innovative services for small and medium-sized enterprises leading exchange.	yes

Create vitality.	no

Benign interaction with high-level security.	no

（德国之声中文网）拜登政府本周五（2月10日）将6个与疑似参与间谍气球计划的中国实体列入黑名单。	(Deutsche Welle Chinese website) The Biden administration on Friday (February 10) blacklisted six Chinese entities suspected of being involved in the spy balloon program.	yes
美国商务部表示，这5家中国公司及1家研究机构帮助中国军队现代化，尤其是航空航天项目，包括飞艇和飞机。	The Commerce Department said the five Chinese companies and one research institute helped modernize China's military, especially aerospace programs, including airships and aircraft.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司很难获得美国的技术出口。	Blacklisted companies have difficulty accessing U.S. technology exports.	yes
名单被称为“实体名单”（entity list），入列的公司除非获得美国商务部的特别出口许可证，否则将无法向美国供应商购买技术或商品。	Known as the "entity list," companies on the list will not be able to buy technology or goods from US suppliers unless they obtain a special export license from the US Department of Commerce.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司是：北京南江空天科技股份有限公司、中国电子科技集团第四十八研究所、东莞凌空遥感科技有限公司、鹰门航空科技集团有限公司、广州天海翔航空科技有限公司和山西鹰门航空科技集团有限公司。	The blacklisted companies are: Beijing Nanjiang Aerospace Technology Co., Ltd., China Electronics Technology Group 48th Research Institute, Dongguan Lingkong Remote Sensing Technology Co., Ltd., Eagle Gate Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd., Guangzhou Tianhaixiang Aviation Technology Co., Ltd. and Shanxi Yingmen Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd.	yes
在此之前，白宫表示考虑做出更广泛措施，“揭露和处理”中国威胁美国国家安全的更大规模监控活动。	Before that, the White House said it was considering broader measures to "expose and address" China's larger surveillance activities that threaten US national security.	yes
气球事件引发中美之间进一步紧张，美国国务卿布林肯取消了访问中国的行程。	The balloon incident sparked further tensions between the US and China, with US Secretary of State Antony Blinken canceling a visit to China.	yes
美国2月4日击落气球，中国政府向美国驻华使馆提出严正交涉，批评美国严重冲击和损害双方稳定中美关系的努力和进程。	The US shot down the balloon on February 4, and the Chinese government lodged stern representations with the US Embassy in China, criticizing the US for seriously impacting and damaging both sides' efforts and process of stabilizing Sino-US relations.	yes
从现有残骸证据及中国军方的采购平台资讯，美国政府得出结论，认为该气球的制造厂商“跟中国解放军有直接关系”，而且是中国军方批准的供应商。	From the evidence of the existing wreckage and information from the Chinese military's procurement platform, the US government concluded that the manufacturer of the balloon "has a direct relationship with the Chinese People's Liberation Army" and is an approved supplier by the Chinese military.	yes
中国外交部发言人毛宁在周五的新闻发布会上表示，关于一只中国无人民用飞艇因不可抗力误入美国领空的意外事件，中方已经多次说明情况、阐明立场。	Chinese Foreign Ministry spokesman Mao Ning said at a press conference on Friday that China has repeatedly explained the situation and clarified its position regarding the accident that a Chinese unmanned civil airship strayed into the U.S. airspace due to force majeure.	yes
根据外交部网站，她补充表示，美国国会的有关决议案纯属政治操弄和炒作。	According to the website of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, she added that the relevant resolution of the US Congress is purely political manipulation and hype.	no
中方对此强烈不满、坚决反对。	China is strongly dissatisfied and firmly opposed to this.	no

60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The world's most destructive earthquake in 60 years	no
智利大地震（1960年）	Chilean Earthquake (1960)	no
当地时间1960年5月22日下午3点11分，智利瓦尔迪维亚发生人类史上观测记录到的规模最大的地震，地震矩规模为9.5。	At 3:11 p.m. local time on May 22, 1960, Valdivia, Chile, experienced the largest earthquake ever observed and recorded in human history, with a magnitude of 9.5.	no
短短十分钟内，瓦尔迪维亚整座城市变为废墟。	In just ten minutes, the entire city of Valdivia was reduced to ruins.	no
地震之后引发的巨大海啸袭击到智利海岸线，掀起浪高高度是25米高的巨大海啸。	The huge tsunami triggered by the earthquake hit the Chilean coastline, setting off a huge tsunami with a wave height of 25 meters.	no
海啸波及到遥远的日本、菲律宾。	The tsunami spread to distant Japan and the Philippines.	no
如此范围的灾难所造成的罹难人数以及经济损失无法精确得知。	The death toll and economic damage from a disaster of this scope cannot be precisely known.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The world's most destructive earthquake in 60 years	no
阿拉斯加大地震（1964年）	Alaska Earthquake (1964)	no
1964年3月27日是一个星期五，也是是耶稣受难日。	March 27, 1964 was a Friday and Good Friday.	no
这一天美国阿拉斯加发生北美洲历史上最大的地震，矩震级达到9.2。	On this day, the largest earthquake in North American history occurred in Alaska, USA, with a moment magnitude of 9.2.	no
直到2006年，阿拉斯加大地震仍然是有纪录以来世界第三大地震。	Until 2006, the Alaska earthquake was the third largest earthquake ever recorded in the world.	no
地震发生时，太平洋板块和北美洲板块之间的一个断层在威廉王子湾接近学院峡湾的地方断裂。	A fault between the Pacific and North American plates ruptured in Prince William Sound near College Sound when the quake struck.	no
在大部分的地区这场地震持续了3分钟到5分钟。	The quake lasted between 3 and 5 minutes in most areas.	no
海床位移引发了巨大的海啸，高度为67米。	The displacement of the sea floor triggered a huge tsunami with a height of 67 meters.	no
由于当天是假日，所以学校和许多企业都关闭了。	Because it was a holiday, schools and many businesses were closed.	no
这场大地震最后导致了139人罹难。	The earthquake killed 139 people.	no
其中9人直接死于地震，其他130人死于地震引发的海啸。	Nine of them died directly from the quake, and 130 others died from the tsunami triggered by the quake.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The world's most destructive earthquake in 60 years	no
唐山大地震（1976年）	Tangshan Earthquake (1976)	no
1976年7月28日，中国河北省唐山市和丰南县在16小时内发生两次7级以上强烈地震。	On July 28, 1976, two strong earthquakes of magnitude 7 or above occurred in Tangshan City and Fengnan County, Hebei Province, China within 16 hours.	no
震源距地面23千米。	The epicenter was 23 kilometers from the ground.	no
唐山市全市交通、通讯、供水、供电中断，顷刻间被夷为平地。	The transportation, communications, water supply, and power supply of Tangshan City were cut off, and they were razed to the ground in an instant.	no
140公里外的首都北京也有强烈震感。	The capital Beijing, 140 kilometers away, was also strongly felt.	no
据官方统计，包括北京、天津在内的所有受灾地区，地震造成242769人死亡，164851人重伤。	According to official statistics, in all affected areas including Beijing and Tianjin, the earthquake caused 242,769 deaths and 164,851 serious injuries.	no
唐山大地震成为中国有记录至今第二多人死亡的地震，仅次于1556年嘉靖大地震。	The Tangshan earthquake became the second deadliest earthquake ever recorded in China, after the Jiajing earthquake in 1556.	no
但是有海外科学家估计，这场地震可能造成至少65万人死亡。	But overseas scientists estimated that the earthquake may have killed at least 650,000 people.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The world's most destructive earthquake in 60 years	no
印度洋大地震（2004年）	Indian Ocean earthquake (2004)	no
2004年12月26日，印尼苏门答腊岛亚齐省西岸160公里处发生地震，震源深度30公里，矩震级9.1到9.3。	On December 26, 2004, an earthquake occurred 160 kilometers away from the west coast of Aceh Province, Sumatra, Indonesia, with a focal depth of 30 kilometers and a moment magnitude of 9.1 to 9.3.	no
地震引发了浪高高度达15到30米的巨大海啸。	The earthquake triggered a huge tsunami with a wave height of 15 to 30 meters.	no
太平洋沿岸总共14个国家被波及，其中受灾严重最严重的地区包括印尼亚齐省、泰国镐立和普吉岛渡假区、斯里兰卡和印度泰米尔邦。	A total of 14 countries along the Pacific Rim have been affected, with the hardest-hit areas including Aceh Province in Indonesia, the resort areas of Khao Lak and Phuket in Thailand, Sri Lanka and Tamil State in India.	no
当时正值圣诞节的旅游旺季，受灾地区聚集了大量的旅客和本地居民，导致许多在沙滩上享受假期的旅客和在海边工作的当地人被海啸卷到海底，使这次地震不少人成为失踪者。	At that time, it was the peak tourist season of Christmas, and a large number of tourists and local residents gathered in the affected area. As a result, many tourists enjoying their holidays on the beach and locals working by the sea were swept to the bottom of the sea by the tsunami, making many people become victims of the earthquake. missing person.	no
据估计，罹难人数和失踪人数至少有30万人。	It is estimated that the number of dead and missing is at least 300,000 people.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The world's most destructive earthquake in 60 years	no
汶川大地震（2008年）	Wenchuan Earthquake (2008)	no
2008年5月12日，中国四川省汶川地区发生大地震。	On May 12, 2008, a major earthquake occurred in Wenchuan, Sichuan Province, China.	no
根据中国地震局的数据，此次地震的面波震级达8.2级、矩震级达8.3级，破坏地区超过10万平方公里。	According to data from the China Earthquake Administration, the surface wave magnitude of the earthquake was 8.2, and the moment magnitude was 8.3, destroying an area of more than 100,000 square kilometers.	no
截至2008年9月25日，地震共计造成69227人遇难，17923人失踪，374643人不同程度受伤，1993.03万人失去住所，受灾总人口达4625.6万人。	As of September 25, 2008, the earthquake had killed 69,227 people, 17,923 were missing, 374,643 were injured to varying degrees, 19,930,300 people lost their homes, and the total affected population reached 46,256,000.	no
是中华人民共和国成立以来破坏力最大的地震，也是唐山大地震后伤亡最惨重的一次。	It was the most destructive earthquake since the founding of the People's Republic of China, and it was also the one with the heaviest casualties after the Tangshan Earthquake.	no
2009年3月，中国国务院宣布将每年的5月12日定为防灾减灾日，加强对民众的教育和对防灾减灾工作的关注。	In March 2009, the State Council of China announced that May 12 of each year will be designated as the Disaster Prevention and Mitigation Day to strengthen public education and attention to disaster prevention and mitigation.	no
之后中国多地政府和中小学在每年这一天举行防震演习。	Afterwards, governments and primary and secondary schools in many places in China hold earthquake drills on this day every year.	no
中小学也开始重视普及“防震减灾”教育。	Primary and secondary schools have also begun to attach importance to the popularization of "earthquake prevention and disaster reduction" education.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The world's most destructive earthquake in 60 years	no
海地地震（2010年）	Haiti Earthquake (2010)	no
2010年1月12日，加勒比海岛国海地发生里氏7.0级的地震。	On January 12, 2010, an earthquake measuring 7.0 on the Richter scale occurred in the Caribbean island country of Haiti.	no
震中位于海地首都太子港以西南方25公里，震源距离地表13千米左右。	The epicenter was located 25 kilometers southwest of the Haitian capital Port-au-Prince, and the epicenter was about 13 kilometers from the surface.	no
国际红十字会估计，受到地震影响的人口大约为300万。	The International Committee of the Red Cross estimates that the number of people affected by the quake is around 3 million.	no
海地政府公布的确认死亡人数超过20万。	The Haitian government has confirmed the death toll at more than 200,000.	no
海地国内的一些地区，多达90%的房屋在地震中被摧毁。	In some parts of Haiti, as many as 90% of houses were destroyed in the earthquake.	no
虽然国际社会提供了大量援助和支持，但是这个人口过剩腐败横行的贫困国家从未从这场灾难中恢复过来。	Despite massive aid and support from the international community, the impoverished, overpopulated, corrupt country never recovered from the devastation.	no

日本东北大地震（2011年）	The Great Tohoku Earthquake in Japan (2011)	no
2011年3月11日日本东北地方外海发生矩震级为9.0的大型逆冲区地震。	On March 11, 2011, a large thrust zone earthquake with a moment magnitude of 9.0 occurred off the coast of Tohoku, Japan.	no
震中位于在宫城县首府仙台市以东的太平洋海域，震源深度测得数据为24千米，并且引发最大爬高40.1米的巨大海啸。	The epicenter of the earthquake was located in the Pacific Ocean east of Sendai City, the capital of Miyagi Prefecture. The measured depth of the epicenter was 24 kilometers, and it triggered a huge tsunami with a maximum height of 40.1 meters.	no
这场地震是日本有观测纪录到以来第一个震级超过9的地震。	The quake was the first recorded in Japan to have a magnitude greater than 9.	no
约有2.2万人在灾害丧生，大约40万座建筑被完全摧毁或倒塌。	About 22,000 people lost their lives in the disaster, and about 400,000 buildings were completely destroyed or collapsed.	no
福岛第一核电站受地震海啸影响发生泄漏事故。	The Fukushima Daiichi Nuclear Power Plant suffered a leak due to the earthquake and tsunami.	no
这次事故在国际核事件分级表（INES）中被分类为最严重的7级。	The accident was classified as level 7, the most severe, on the International Nuclear Event Scale (INES).	no
福岛核事故导致在全世界都测量到微量辐射性物质，包括碘-131、铯-137（半衰期为30年）在内。	The Fukushima nuclear accident led to the measurement of trace amounts of radioactive substances all over the world, including iodine-131 and cesium-137 (with a half-life of 30 years).	no
大量放射性同位素因此核事故释入太平洋。	Large quantities of radioactive isotopes were released into the Pacific Ocean as a result of the nuclear accident.	no
根据联合国的统计，在土叙两国灾区，目前至少有87万人急需食物。	According to the statistics of the United Nations, at least 870,000 people in the disaster-stricken areas of Turkey and Syria are in urgent need of food.	no
仅仅在叙利亚，就有多达530万人因为地震而失去家园。	In Syria alone, as many as 5.3 million people lost their homes due to the earthquake.	no

目前灾区气温低至零下，很多灾民没有住所。	At present, the temperature in the disaster area is as low as zero, and many victims have no shelter.	no

在地震发生后的四天内，世界粮食计划署已经向土耳其和叙利亚的11.5万人提供了食物救济。	In the four days since the earthquake, the World Food Program has provided food relief to 115,000 people in Turkey and Syria.	no

NEWS GOV-MO: 警情通告：司警局呼吁市民提防假冒电讯公司诈骗短讯	NEWS GOV-MO: Police Notice: The Judiciary Police Department appeals to the public to beware of fraudulent text messages from counterfeit telecommunications companies	yes
近日司警局接获多宗电信诈骗案，不法分子假冒本澳电讯公司向事主发送附有网站连结的诈骗短信，以积分到期须尽快换领奖赏为饵，诱骗事主登入虚假网站进行兑换。	Recently, the Judiciary Police Department has received a number of telecommunications fraud cases. The criminals pretended to be local telecommunications companies and sent fraudulent text messages with website links to the victims. They lured the victims to log on to fake websites for redemption with the bait of redeeming rewards as soon as possible when the points expired.	yes
事主按指示输入信用卡资料及验证码，随即收到金融机构通知信用卡出现不明消费记录，怀疑信用卡资料经上述网站被盗取。	The victim entered the credit card information and verification code according to the instructions, and then received a notice from the financial institution that the credit card had an unknown consumption record. He suspected that the credit card information was stolen through the above-mentioned website.	yes
经查，证实相关电讯公司并无发出上述短讯。	After investigation, it was confirmed that the relevant telecommunications company did not send the above-mentioned short message.	yes
司警局呼吁市民，如接获类似手机短讯须提高警惕，切勿登入短讯所载网站连结或提供任何个人资料；若被要求提供信用卡资料、帐户交易密码、交易验证码，更要加倍谨慎，防止信用卡被盗刷。	The Judiciary Police Department appeals to the public to be more vigilant if they receive similar mobile phone text messages, and do not log in to the website links contained in the text messages or provide any personal information; if they are asked to provide credit card information, account transaction passwords, and transaction verification codes, doubly be cautious to prevent credit card fraud.	yes
防骗提示：	Anti-fraud tips:	yes
1. 多关注网络安全资讯，提高个人防范意识；	1. Pay more attention to network security information and improve personal awareness of prevention;	yes
2. 切勿随便登入来历不明的网站并在网站内登记个人及信用卡资料，以防遭人盗用；	2. Do not log in to websites from unknown sources and register personal and credit card information in the website to prevent misappropriation;	yes
3. 警惕假冒网站及钓鱼网站，时刻留意网站网址是否与官方网站完全相符；	3. Be wary of fake websites and phishing websites, and always pay attention to whether the website URL is exactly the same as the official website;	yes
4. 为手机、移动装置或电脑安装防毒软件，并定期更新；	4. Install anti-virus software for mobile phones, mobile devices or computers, and update them regularly;	yes
5. 怀疑遇到诈骗或其他犯罪时，应立即致电司警局防诈骗查询热线8800 7777或报案热线993求助。	5. When you suspect fraud or other crimes, you should immediately call the anti-fraud inquiry hotline 8800 7777 or the reporting hotline 993 of the Judiciary Police for help.	no

The two-day (10th and 11th) schedule included working meetings and industry talks, and Hong Kong travel agency industry and media representatives visited many tourist attractions, hotels and tourism-related facilities in Macau in batches to introduce the latest Macau tourism products to the Hong Kong market, and at the same time promote the linkage of cultural tourism between the two places, and jointly expand the market of "connected travel" between Hong Kong and Macau.	yes
亲临考察引入澳门旅游新玩法	Introduce a new way of tourism in Macau	yes
是次香港百人大型考察团包括香港政府旅游相关部门领导主管、60多位来自旅行社及港澳跨境交通营运商的代表以及约30位分别来自旅游杂志及报章的记者、旅游社交媒体、网络媒体代表及博客/网红等，亲临澳门交流考察，了解澳门最新旅游资源，香港业界及媒体将澳门旅游的新玩法带给香港居民以至访港旅客，藉香港交通枢纽的优势，拓展港澳“联线同游”市场。	The 100-person large-scale Hong Kong delegation includes leaders of tourism-related departments of the Hong Kong government, more than 60 representatives from travel agencies and cross-border transportation operators from Hong Kong and Macau, and about 30 reporters from travel magazines and newspapers, travel social media, Internet media representatives and bloggers/Internet celebrities, etc., to visit Macau for exchanges and investigations to learn about the latest tourism resources in Macau. The Hong Kong industry and media will bring new ways of traveling in Macau to Hong Kong residents and tourists, and take advantage of Hong Kong's transportation hub to expand the market of "connected travel" between Hong Kong and Macau.	yes

（综合11日电）	(Comprehensive 11th)	yes

”Bard在回答中提到该望远镜曾拍摄到太阳系外行星的第一张照片。	In his answer, Bard mentioned that the telescope had taken the first photo of an exoplanet.	yes

新加坡旅游业复苏强劲 入境旅客比2021年增长19倍	Singapore tourism recovers strongly, arrivals up 19 times compared to 2021	yes
（综合11日电）新加坡旅游局近日公布，预计2023年到访新加坡的国际旅客人次可达1200万至1400万，将带来约180亿至210亿新元的旅游收益；旅客人次和旅游收入将恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约67%至75%的水平；2024年旅游业实现全面复苏的可能性很大。	(Comprehensive, 11th) The Singapore Tourism Board recently announced that it is estimated that the number of international tourists visiting Singapore in 2023 will reach 12 million to 14 million, which will bring about 18 billion to 21 billion Singapore dollars in tourism revenue; the number of tourists and tourism revenue will return to the level of about 67% to 75% before the new crown epidemic in 2019; the possibility of a full recovery of the tourism industry in 2024 is very high.	yes
2022年新加坡旅游市场逐步重新启动和恢复。	In 2022, the Singapore tourism market will gradually restart and recover.	yes
新加坡旅游局最新发布的统计数据显示，2022年入境旅客从2021年的33.06万人次增长19倍，达到630万人次，超越旅游局早前预估的400万至600万人次，游客已经恢复至疫情前33%的水平。	According to the latest statistics released by the Singapore Tourism Board, the number of inbound tourists in 2022 will increase 19 times from 330,600 in 2021 to 6.3 million, surpassing the tourism bureau's previous estimate of 4 million to 6 million. Tourists have recovered from the epidemic. The top 33% level.	yes
2022年1月至9月，新加坡旅游收入共计89.6亿新元，预计2022年全年旅游收入可达138亿至143亿新元，比2021年的18.9亿新元增长6倍至7倍，已经恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约50%至52%的水平。	From January to September 2022, Singapore's tourism revenue totaled 8.96 billion Singapore dollars. It is estimated that the annual tourism revenue in 2022 will reach 13.8 billion to 14.3 billion Singapore dollars, an increase of 6 to 7 times compared with 1.89 billion Singapore dollars in 2021. Return to the level of about 50% to 52% before the new crown epidemic in 2019.	yes

旅游局日前宣布，将计划在未来两年从这笔预算中拨出1.1亿新元，推出更多商业和休闲活动吸引旅客回流。	The Tourism Bureau announced a few days ago that it plans to allocate 110 million Singapore dollars from this budget in the next two years to launch more commercial and leisure activities to attract tourists to return.	yes

新加坡旅游局体育与康养旅游执行署长王凌丽说，近年来，越来越多的游客把身体健康放在各项考虑因素的首位。	Wang Lingli, executive director of sports and wellness tourism of the Singapore Tourism Board, said that in recent years, more and more tourists put their health at the top of all considerations.	yes

重阳问答︱如何看待美国1月非农就业数据大超预期及未来趋势 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	Chongyang Q&A - How to view the US non-agricultural employment data in January exceeded expectations and future trends - Economic Observation Network - Professional Financial News Website	yes
Q：请问重阳投资，如何看待美国1月非农就业数据大超预期及未来趋势？	Q: May I ask Chongyang Investment, what do you think of the US non-agricultural employment data in January exceeding expectations and the future trend?	yes
A：2月3日美国劳工部公布2023年1月非农就业数据，新增非农就业51.7万人，大幅高于市场预期的18.9万人；失业率降至3.4%，为近50年以来的最低位；时薪同比增速4.4%，环比增速0.3%，略有放缓。	A: On February 3, the U.S. Department of Labor announced the non-agricultural employment data for January 2023. New non-agricultural employment was 517,000, much higher than the market expectation of 189,000; the unemployment rate fell to 3.4%, the lowest level in the past 50 years; hourly wages increased by 4.4% year-on-year and 0.3% month-on-month, a slight slowdown.	yes
从总量上来看，本次数据存在很多一次性和技术性因素的扰动，比如罢工返岗的教职工、调查统计口径的修正、季调因子的更新，后续可能将有所修正（参考2022年1月新增非农由50.4万人下修至36.4万人），非农就业或不像数据体现的那样强劲。	From the perspective of the total amount, there are many one-time and technical disturbances in the data this time, such as the faculty and staff returning to work on strike, the revision of the survey statistics, and the update of the seasonal adjustment factor, which may be revised in the future (refer to 2022 1 The increase in non-agricultural employment was revised down from 504,000 to 364,000), and non-agricultural employment may not be as strong as the data suggests.	yes
从结构上来看，高科技企业裁员影响仍在，但占比较低；高接触性服务业如休闲酒店、教育保健等新增就业大幅回升，数据显示服务业劳动力缺口仍存。	From a structural point of view, the impact of layoffs in high-tech companies is still there, but the proportion is relatively low; new employment in high-touch service industries such as leisure hotels, education and health care has rebounded sharply, and data shows that there is still a labor gap in the service industry.	yes
结合同样大超预期的服务业PMI、岗位空缺和劳动力缺口数据的回升和消费信贷数据的强势，我们判断经过极端天气和节假日后美国服务业迎来了快速修复。	Combined with the rebound in service industry PMI, job vacancies and labor gap data, which also exceeded expectations, and the strength of consumer credit data, we judge that the US service industry has ushered in a quick recovery after extreme weather and holidays.	yes
我们认为，在不经过衰退的情况下美国就业市场的供需紧张难以改善。	We believe that the tight supply and demand in the US job market will hardly improve without going through a recession.	yes
目前美国劳动力市场尚有500余万的供给缺口，而劳动参与率上行缓慢，尤其是25-54岁劳动参与率已经接近疫情前高点。	At present, there is still a supply gap of more than 5 million in the US labor market, while the labor force participation rate is rising slowly, especially the labor force participation rate of 25-54 years old is close to the pre-epidemic high.	yes
除此之外，由于美国居民超额储蓄和消费信贷的强势，消费需求的强劲将促使紧缩政策对就业市场的影响进一步滞后。	In addition, due to the strength of excess savings of American residents and consumer credit, strong consumer demand will further lag the impact of tightening policies on the job market.	yes
美国就业市场供需持续紧张将是2023年美国经济的底色。	The continued tight supply and demand in the U.S. job market will be the background of the U.S. economy in 2023.	yes

However, the market has turned a blind eye to the Fed's hawkish statement. It not only expects to stop raising interest rates early, but also expects two cut interest rates.	no
在劳动力市场供需紧张，紧缩政策影响不明的情况下，我们认为美联储年末对于加息的指引是相对合理的，市场极端预期的调整和交易的拥挤或将对市场产生一定伤害。	In the context of tight supply and demand in the labor market and unclear impacts of tightening policies, we believe that the Fed's guidance on raising interest rates at the end of the year is relatively reasonable, and the adjustment of extreme market expectations and crowded transactions may cause some damage to the market.	no
尽管如此，薪资增速的顽固难改当前通胀快速下降的趋势，随着M2数据同比转负以及各个CPI分项领先指标的逐渐转好，自10月份以来美国CPI数据已经转向快速下降阶段，薪资增速的顽固仅会对以后的通胀数据形成托底，当前的市场预期难以证伪，在下一期通胀数据公布后市场或进入新一轮博弈。	Nevertheless, the stubbornness of wage growth cannot change the current trend of rapid decline in inflation. The stubbornness of wage growth will only form a foundation for future inflation data. The current market expectations are difficult to falsify. 杉杉创始人郑永刚因突发心脏疾病过世 曾带领中国服装第一股转型 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	Zheng Yonggang, the founder of Shanshan, died of a heart attack	yes
经济观察网 记者 郑淯心 2月11日，认证主体为杉杉控股有限公司（以下简称“杉杉控股 ” ） 的微信公众号发布讣告，杉杉企业创始人、杉杉控股董事局主席郑永刚因突发心脏疾病救治无效，于2023年2月10日去世，享年65岁。	Economic Observation Network reporter Zheng Yuxin On February 11, the WeChat public account of Shanshan Holding Co., Ltd. (hereinafter referred to as "Shanshan Holding") issued an obituary. Zheng Yonggang, the founder of Shanshan Enterprise and chairman of the board of directors of Shanshan Holding, died on February 10, 2023 at the age of 65 due to ineffective treatment for heart disease.	yes
上世纪80年代，郑永刚担任国营棉纺厂的厂长，随着调任，1989年郑永刚成为杉杉股份的前身宁波云港服装总厂的厂长。	In the 1980s, Zheng Yonggang served as the factory director of the state-owned cotton spinning factory. After being transferred, Zheng Yonggang became the factory director of Ningbo Yungang Garment Factory, the predecessor of Shanshan Co., Ltd. in 1989.	yes
2022年12月，在第二十届中国企业领袖年会暨第二十二届中国企业未来之星年会上，郑永刚在演讲中称，在上世纪90年代的中国西服市场，杉杉品牌的市占率曾高达37 % 。	In December 2022, at the 20th Annual Meeting of Chinese Enterprise Leaders and the 22nd Annual Meeting of Future Stars of Chinese Enterprises, Zheng Yonggang said in his speech that in the Chinese suit market in the 1990s, the Shanshan brand accounted for 37% of the market.	yes
1996年杉杉股份（600884.SH）上市，成为中国服装业第一家上市公司。	In 1996, Shanshan Co., Ltd. (600884.SH) went public, becoming the first listed company in China's garment industry.	yes
就在服装业务如日中天时，杉杉集团却开始转型，因为郑永刚意识到 ， “ 一旦市场放开，中国品牌自然会形成一个梯队式品牌市场，杉杉西服想一直独领风骚，长期成为国人的国服的可能性不大 ” 。	Just when the clothing business was in full swing, Shanshan Group began to transform, because Zheng Yonggang realized, "Once the market is liberalized, Chinese brands will naturally form an echelon brand market, Shanshan suits want to always lead the way, it is unlikely to become the national service of Chinese people in the long term."	yes
1999年，杉杉开始研究企业转型，郑永刚回忆当年 ， “ 我们来到上海，寻求到底转型做什么，专门找了很多专家学者，连续不断地开一些诸葛亮会、务虚研讨会。	In 1999, Shanshan began to study enterprise transformation. Zheng Yonggang recalled that year, "We came to Shanghai to find out what to do in transformation. We specially found many experts and scholars, and held some Zhuge Liang meetings and retreat seminars continuously.	yes
最后，我们设定了两个大的战略方向。	Finally, we set two major strategic directions.	yes
第一个方向是新能源新材料，另外一个是大健康有未来 ” 。	The first direction is new energy and new materials, and the other is that great health has a future."	yes
战略方向确定后，杉杉开始寻找合作，那时候鞍山热能院为鞍钢配套的炭素研究所在做国家863课题，科研经费不够，于是杉杉和鞍山热能院碳素研究所签署合作协议，共同推动国家863课题“中间相炭微球”项目产业化，从事负极材料的研发、生产和销售，在国内实现负极材料的商用推广。	After the strategic direction was determined, Shanshan began to look for cooperation. At that time, Anshan Institute of Thermal Energy's carbon research institute supporting Ansteel was working on the national 863 project, and the research funds were not enough, so Shanshan signed a cooperation agreement with the carbon research institute of Anshan Thermal Energy Institute to jointly promote the industrialization of the national 863 project "mesophase carbon microspheres" project, engaged in the research and development, production and sales of negative electrode materials, and realized the commercial promotion of negative electrode materials in China.	yes
2001年，杉杉股份实现中间相炭微球的规模化生产，开始国产化替代，取代日本成为国内中间相炭微球主要供应商。	In 2001, Shanshan Co., Ltd. realized the large-scale production of mesocarbon microspheres, and began to replace Japan as the main supplier of mesocarbon microspheres in China.	no
这是中国第一家锂离子电池负极材料生产企业，实现了锂离子电池负极材料国产化。	This is the first lithium-ion battery anode material manufacturer in China, realizing the localization of lithium-ion battery anode materials.	no
随着锂电池的应用迅速普及，杉杉股份的锂电池业务开始逐步发展，2007年锂电材料业务被写入了杉杉股份的主营业务，服装业务营收占比逐年减少，直至2013年，杉杉股份的锂电材料业务收入全面超过服装业务。	With the rapid popularization of the application of lithium batteries, the lithium battery business of Shanshan Co., Ltd. began to develop gradually. In 2007, the lithium battery material business was included in the main business of Shanshan Co., Ltd., and the proportion of clothing business revenue decreased year by year until 2013. Shanshan's lithium battery material business has more revenue than its clothing business.	no
2021年2月，杉杉股份成功并购LG化学偏光片业务，进军LCD偏光片市场，并成立偏光片企业杉金光电，该领域技术含量比较高，杉杉的主要的竞争对手都是世界500强，如韩国三星、日本的住友化学、日东电工。	In February 2021, Shanshan Co., Ltd. successfully acquired LG Chem's polarizer business, entered the LCD polarizer market, and established Shanjin Optoelectronics, a polarizer company. This field has relatively high technology content. Shanshan's main competitors are all Fortune 500 companies, such as South Korea's Samsung, Japan's Sumitomo Chemical, and Nitto Denko.	no
郑永刚曾分享过投后管理的心得 ， “ 中国的民营企业收购国际上的一些高科技企业，成功概率比较低，为什么那些收购会失败？	Zheng Yonggang once shared his experience in post-investment management, "The probability of success for Chinese private enterprises to acquire some international high-tech companies is relatively low. Why do those acquisitions fail?	no
因为大家都会去考虑，我花了那么多钱，我得去派人管对吧，这是通常会做的一个行为 ” ， 然而郑永刚则不同，杉杉收购成功的那一天，郑永刚就到杉金光电当众宣布，杉杉作为杉金的大股东，决定实施一企两制，除了郑永刚担任董事长，杉杉企业的人不派到杉金，采取授权经营的方式，原有的分配制度、企业文化、各项管理等模式不变。	Because everyone will think about it, I have spent so much money, I have to send someone to take care of it, right? This is a common behavior." However, Zheng Yonggang is different. On the day Shanshan's acquisition was successful, Zheng Yonggang went to Shanshan Optoelectronics publicly announced that Shanshan, as the major shareholder of Shanjin, decided to implement one enterprise, two systems. Except for Zheng Yonggang as the chairman, Shanshan Enterprises will not send people to Shanjin, and adopt the method of authorization. The original distribution system, corporate culture, management and other models remain unchanged.	no
ICC鑫椤资讯发布2022年负极数据显示，杉杉负极2022年出货量突破20万吨，同比增幅100 % ， 市场份额达16 % ， 人造石墨负极材料出货量蝉联榜首。	ICC Xinyu Information released the negative electrode data for 2022, showing that Shanshan's negative electrode shipments in 2022 will exceed 200,000 tons, a year-on-year increase of 100%, and its market share will reach 16%. The shipment of artificial graphite negative electrode materials will continue to top the list.	no
在偏光片业务方面，Yano Research统计显示，公司旗下杉金光电2022年全球市场份额达到29 % ， 预计2023年市场份额将达到32 % ， 持续位列全球第一。	In terms of polarizer business, statistics from Yano Research show that the company's Shanjin Optoelectronics will have a global market share of 29% in 2022 and is expected to reach 32% in 2023, continuing to rank first in the world.	no

“基金E账户”来了：证监会授权开发 投资者名下所有基金实现归集和查询 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	"Fund E Account" is here: China Securities Regulatory Commission authorizes the development of all funds under the investor's name to achieve collection and query - Economic Observation Network - Professional Financial News Website	yes
经济观察网 记者 陈姗 基金购买渠道繁杂导致账户信息归集不易？	Economic Observation Network reporter Chen Shan Does the complexity of fund purchase channels make it difficult to collect account information?	yes
总是遗忘“小金库”？	Always forget the "little treasury"?	yes
基民的这些问题即将得到解决。	These problems of Christianity are about to be solved.	yes
2月10日，证监会公告称，“基金E账户”APP在各手机应用商店上架并开展公开试运行。	On February 10, the China Securities Regulatory Commission announced that the "Fund E Account" APP was put on the shelves of various mobile phone application stores and launched a public trial run.	yes
据介绍，“基金E账户”为个人投资者提供公募基金账户及份额信息的“一站式”查询服务，旨在解决广大中小投资者遗忘账户、查询繁琐等行业服务痛点。	According to reports, the "Fund E Account" provides individual investors with a "one-stop" query service for public fund accounts and share information, aiming to solve industry service pain points such as forgetting accounts and cumbersome inquiries for small and medium investors.	yes
据Wind数据显示，截至2022年底，国内共有公募基金管理人156家，管理基金规模约26万亿元；公募基金份额登记机构167家，公募基金销售机构411家。	According to Wind data, as of the end of 2022, there are 156 public fund managers in China, with a fund management scale of about 26 trillion yuan; 167 public fund share registration agencies, and 411 public fund sales agencies.	yes
各份额登记机构账户体系相互独立，缺乏行业统一的查询渠道。	The account systems of each share registration agency are independent of each other, and there is no unified inquiry channel for the industry.	yes
有行业人士表示，2021年末我国基金投资者超过7.2亿人，也就是说，全国有一半人都投资了基金产品。	Some people in the industry said that by the end of 2021, there will be more than 720 million fund investors in China, which means that half of the people in the country have invested in fund products.	yes
此前，投资者需要通过不同销售机构查询购买情况，而通过“基金E账户”可以查询所有销售渠道购买的情况，持有基金情况一目了然。	Previously, investors needed to inquire about the purchase status through different sales agencies, but through the "fund E account," they can inquire about the purchase status of all sales channels, and the fund holding status is clear at a glance.	yes
“基金E账户”APP是什么？	What is the "Fund E Account" APP?	no
据相关文件介绍，“基金E账户”APP 是中国结算经中国证监会批准开发建设的公募基金行业门户手机应用，可为投资者提供全市场公募基金产品场外份额持有情况的一站式查询。	According to relevant documents, the "Fund E Account" APP is a public offering fund industry portal mobile application developed and constructed by China Settlement with the approval of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, which can provide investors with one-stop inquiries on the off-market share holdings of public offering fund products in the whole market.	no
投资者可以通过“基金E账户”方便、快捷地掌握自己通过全市场各销售渠道购买的各基金管理人旗下公募基金产品场外份额的持有情况，全面提升查询效率。	Investors can use the "Fund E Account" to conveniently and quickly grasp the holdings of the off-market shares of the public offering fund products of each fund manager purchased by them through various sales channels in the whole market, and comprehensively improve the query efficiency.	no
具体来说，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”查询到的信息包括：在全市场各公募基金管理人处开立的基金账户信息、在公募基金销售机构处开立的交易账户信息以及持有的包括公开募集证券投资基金以及证券公司设立管理的投资者人数不受200人限制的集合资产管理计划等产品的场外份额持有情况。	Specifically, the information that investors can query through the "Fund E Account" includes: information on fund accounts opened with managers of public funds in the market, information on trading accounts opened at sales agencies of public funds, and information on holdings of off-market share holdings of products including publicly offered securities investment funds and collective asset management plans established and managed by securities companies with no limit of 200 investors.	no
上海证券基金评价研究中心业务负责人刘亦千向经济观察网记者表示，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”App一站式获知其所有的场外公募基金持有情况，帮助其找回“被遗忘的资产”，更重要的是为客户实现了综合基金投资情况的全账户信息归集，帮助客户更及时、准确、完整的掌握自身投资情况，从而更好地优化自身的基金组合配置，更好地规划自身的财务安排。	Liu Yiqian, business director of the Shanghai Securities Fund Evaluation and Research Center, told the Economic Observer.com reporter that investors can use the "Fund E Account" app to know all of their off-market public offering fund holdings in one stop and help them find "forgotten assets." More importantly, it has realized the collection of comprehensive fund investment information for customers, helping customers to grasp their own investment conditions in a more timely, accurate and complete manner, so as to better optimize their fund portfolio allocation and better plan their own financial arrangements.	no
如何注册使用？	How to register to use?	no
记者注意到，目前，“基金E账户”APP已在华为、苹果、小米、OPPO、vivo等手机应用商店上架，但APP尚处于公开试运行阶段，注册需要填写邀请码，投资者可以联系所持有基金的基金管理人获取。	The reporter noticed that at present, the "Fund E Account" APP has been put on the shelves of mobile application stores such as Huawei, Apple, Xiaomi, OPPO, vivo, etc., but the APP is still in the stage of public trial operation. Registration requires filling in the invitation code. Investors can contact the fund manager holding the fund to obtain it.	no
上海一家中大型公募基金客服人员向经济观察网记者提供了一个6位数的邀请码，并告诉记者，“APP试运行阶段，中国结算提供给每个基金管理人一定数量的邀请码，投资者电话过来获取，我们都会提供。	The customer service staff of a medium and large public offering fund in Shanghai provided a 6-digit invitation code to the reporter of Economic Observer.com, and told the reporter, "During the trial operation of the APP, China Settlement provided a certain number of invitation codes to each fund manager. Call and get it, and we'll provide it.	no
等试运行结束后，开放用户注册时就不用邀请码了。	After the trial run is over, the invitation code will not be needed when opening user registration.	no
”	"	no
记者根据证监会官网公示的“基金E账户”下载及使用说明相关文件进行了账户注册并完成查询，整个过程耗时仅几分钟，主要分为四步：用户注册、实名认证、基金账户绑定、公募基金查询。	The reporter registered the account and completed the query according to the download of the "Fund E Account" published on the official website of the China Securities Regulatory Commission and the relevant documents for use. The whole process took only a few minutes and was mainly divided into four steps: user registration, real-name authentication, fund account binding, public offering fund inquiries.	no
通过实名认证这一步之后，点击“资产”基金绑定按钮，记者通过各个基金销售平台购买的所有基金产品都呈现在绑定选项列表中（可绑定账户），完成绑定后就可以直观看到所投基金总资产并可以开始使用查询功能了。	After passing the real-name authentication step, click the "assets" fund binding button, and all the fund products purchased by the reporter through various fund sales platforms will be displayed in the binding option list (account can be bound), and you can see the total assets of the invested fund directly after the binding is completed and you can start using the query function.	no
值得注意的是，“基金E账户”仅为投资者提供查询服务，并不能进行申赎买卖。	It is worth noting that the "Fund E Account" only provides inquiry services for investors, and cannot be used for redemption and trading.	no
“基金 E 账户”所显示的数据日期一般为用户进行查询的日期（T日)往前推三个交易日。	The date of data displayed in the "Fund E Account" is generally three trading days before the date of the user's query (T day).	no
比如，在2 月10日打开“基金E账户”，资产页所显示的总资产、基金份额、基金净值对应日期为该日期往前推三个交易日，即2月7日。	For example, if you open the "Fund E Account" on February 10, the corresponding date of the total assets, fund shares, and fund net value displayed on the asset page is three trading days before that date, that is, February 7.	no

中国鼓励拉高生育率 到高校催捐精 质量高标准	China encourages the increase of fertility rate, urges sperm donation to colleges and universities, high quality standards	yes
中国云南省人类精子库9日发出宣传，征求大专以上学历者或在校生捐精，成功捐赠8至12次可获人民币4500元补贴。	The Human Sperm Bank of China's Yunnan Province issued a promotion on the 9th, soliciting sperm donations from those with a college degree or above or school students. If you successfully donate 8 to 12 times, you will receive a subsidy of RMB 4,500.	yes
据台媒今天报道称，该讯息当日冲上微博热搜，并引发浙江、陕西、湖北、山东与北京等许多省市跟进倡议。	According to Taiwan media reports today, the news rushed to Weibo hot searches that day, and triggered follow-up initiatives in many provinces and cities such as Zhejiang, Shaanxi, Hubei, Shandong and Beijing.	yes

捐精者条件包括，身高165公分以上、大专及以上学历或在读，无色盲色弱、B肝等遗传疾病与传染病者。	The requirements for sperm donors include those with a height of 165 cm or more, a college degree or above or those who are studying, without color blindness, color weakness, hepatitis B and other genetic diseases and infectious diseases.	yes

东德最后一位共产党总理今去世	East Germany's last communist chancellor dies today	yes
东德共产党的继任者在该党在一份声明中报告，“昨晚，汉斯·莫德罗 (Hans Modrow) 离开了我们，享年 95 岁。	The party's successor to the East German Communist Party reported in a statement, "Last night, Hans Modrow left us at the age of 95.	yes
因此，我们的党失去了一位重要领导人。	As a result, our party has lost an important leader.	yes
”	"	yes
1989 年 11 月 13 日，在将东柏林和西柏林分开 28 年的柏林墙打开四天后，莫德罗曾表示他将帮助把东德变成一个民主国家。	On November 13, 1989, four days after the opening of the Berlin Wall that had separated East and West Berlin for 28 years, Modelo had said he would help turn East Germany into a democracy.	yes
当时，由于东德各地的抗议者要求民主和自由，共产党领导人被迫下台。	At the time, Communist leaders were forced to step down as protesters across East Germany demanded democracy and freedom.	yes
戈尔巴乔夫 (Mikhail Gorbachev) 在苏联上台后曾要求在苏联主导的东欧也进行变革。	When the Soviet Union came to power, Mikhail Gorbachev demanded changes in Soviet-dominated Eastern Europe as well.	yes
1990 年 3 月，莫德罗宣布德意志民主共和国 (GDR) 的第一次也是唯一一次自由选举。	In March 1990, Modelo declared the first and only free elections in the German Democratic Republic (GDR).	yes
选举结果导致他不再担任总理。	The election results resulted in him no longer serving as prime minister.	yes
尽管莫德罗进行了改革，但反对者指责他试图推迟 1990 年 10 月发生的政治变革和统一。	Despite Modelo's reforms, opponents accused him of trying to delay the political change and unification that took place in October 1990.	yes
他还因试图重塑而不是废除秘密警察而受到批评。	He has also been criticized for trying to reshape rather than abolish the secret police.	no
1993 年，莫德罗在 1989 年 5 月的市政选举中被判选举舞弊罪名成立，但并未入狱。	In 1993, Modelo was convicted of electoral fraud in the May 1989 municipal elections, but did not go to jail.	no
有称这些指控是出于政治动机。	Some say the charges are politically motivated.	no
1990 年至 1994 年，莫德罗继续在德国议会任职，并于 1999 年至 2004 年担任欧洲议会议员。	Modelo went on to serve in the German parliament from 1990 to 1994 and as a member of the European Parliament from 1999 to 2004.	no
莫德罗将自己视为一名改革者，并希望从内部改变共产党。	Modelo sees himself as a reformer and wants to change the party from within.	no
1999 年，他告诉路透社，他不希望旧东德回归，但表示应该承认东德的成就。	In 1999, he told Reuters he did not want the old East Germany to return but said it should be recognized for its achievements.	no
莫德罗于 1928 年出生在当时的德国小镇 Jasenitz（现为波兰的 Jasienica），并接受过机械师培训。	Modelo was born in 1928 in what was then the German town of Jasenitz (now Jasienica, Poland) and trained as a machinist.	no
第二次世界大战期间，他担任青年消防队排长，并在冲突快结束时成为纳粹民兵组织 Volkssturm 的一员，该组织征召 16 至 60 岁的男子参加最后的战争挣扎。	During World War II, he served as a platoon leader in a youth fire brigade and towards the end of the conflict became a member of the Volkssturm, a Nazi militia organization that recruited men between the ages of 16 and 60 to fight in the last struggles of the war.	no

阿拉斯加上空被击落的 “物体”究竟是什么？	What exactly was the "object" shot down over Alaska?	yes
扑朔迷离，猜测纷纷	confusing, guesswork	yes
美国军方周五（2月10日）下午再次动用美国最先进的隐身喷气战机F-22击落了一个在美国阿拉斯加上空飞行的尚未确定身份的物体。	The US military once again used its most advanced stealth fighter jet, the F-22, to shoot down an unidentified object flying over Alaska, US, on Friday afternoon (February 10).	yes
击落的地点距离阿拉斯加海岸十英里。	It was shot down ten miles off the coast of Alaska.	yes
这是美军在不到一周的时间里第二次击落空中飞行物体。	This is the second time in less than a week that the U.S. military has shot down an airborne object.	yes
上周六，来自中国的一个间谍气球在美国领空上漂移数日后在美国南卡罗莱纳州沿岸附近上空被击毁。	A spy balloon from China was shot down near the coast of South Carolina after days of drifting in U.S. airspace on Saturday.	yes
五角大楼说，第二个被击落的物体于周四晚上首次进入美国领空，在阿拉斯加东北部上空移动时被美国军方跟踪，飞行高度为1.2万米（4万英尺），其大小与一辆小型汽车差不多，与先前被击落的那个中国间谍气球相比要小很多。	The second downed object entered U.S. airspace for the first time Thursday night and was tracked by the U.S. military as it moved over northeast Alaska at an altitude of 12,000 meters (40,000 feet), the Pentagon said. The car is about the same, much smaller than the Chinese spy balloon that was shot down earlier.	yes
五角大楼还认为，目前没有迹象显示，这个物体是可操纵的。	The Pentagon also believes there is currently no indication that the object is manipulable.	yes
白宫国家安全委员会战略沟通协调员约翰·科比周五表示，虽然这个在高空飞行的物体的具体样子尚不清楚，但它“对民航飞机的安全构成了合理的威胁”。	White House National Security Council strategic communications coordinator John Kirby said Friday that while the high-flying object's exact appearance was unclear, it "posed a legitimate threat to the safety of civilian aircraft."	yes
科比表示，这个物体与美国境内发现的那个间谍气球不同，它上面没有悬挂“有效载荷”。	Bryant said the object, unlike the spy balloon found in the United States, did not have a "payload" suspended from it.	yes
科比说，“我们把它称为一个‘物体’是我们目前能够作出的最好的描述”。	"What we call it an'object' is the best description we can currently make," Bryant said.	no
拜登总统在下令击落这个物体之前听取了五角大楼的建议，他作出这个决定的时候“非常谨慎”，科比补充说。	President Biden took the Pentagon's advice before ordering the object down, a decision he made "very carefully," Bryant added.	no
美国官方对这个物体的描述大致可以归纳为：大小相当于一辆小汽车，没有操纵杆，没有悬挂装置，飞行高度为一万米左右。	The US official description of this object can be roughly summarized as follows: the size is equivalent to a small car, there is no joystick, no suspension device, and the flying height is about 10,000 meters.	no
但这些信息还无法回答基本问题，比如这个物体究竟是什么东西，它属于哪个国家，它在执行什么任务。	But this information cannot yet answer basic questions, such as what the object really is, which country it belongs to, and what mission it is performing.	no
